### [1] [Cross-Modal Hierarchical Fusion for from Multi-Sensor Ground Observation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30647)
*Xinze Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AtmoFuseNet融合多视角天空相机图像与毫米波云雷达、云高仪观测，实现4D云状态和风场的密集体积重建。该方法包括跨模态层次聚合、条件变分精炼和基于相关性的运动估计三个阶段，显著提升了液态水含量和风速的估计精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有地面仪器观测数据在模态和空间覆盖上存在异质性，导致云微物理场的密集体积重建仍是一个开放问题。需要一种有效的方法来融合多源异构数据以提高重建精度。

Method: 采用跨模态层次聚合模块，通过层间交叉注意力将图像特征金字塔与仪器垂直剖面结合；使用条件变分精炼模块，在可微雷达和图像前向模型下生成物理一致的微物理场；并通过相关性运动估计模块，从连续体积重建中恢复每体素的3D风矢量。

Result: 在半干旱站点的共位观测数据上，液态水含量平均绝对误差（MAE）为0.026 g m^-3，风速MAE为1.18 m s^-1，优于现有基线方法。消融实验验证了各模块的有效性。

Conclusion: AtmoFuseNet成功实现了多源异构观测数据的高效融合，显著提升了云微物理场和风场的4D重建精度，具有良好的应用前景。

Abstract: Dense volumetric reconstruction of cloud microphysical fields from sparse ground-based instruments remains an open problem, largely because the available measurements are heterogeneous in both modality and spatial coverage. We present AtmoFuseNet, a framework that fuses multi-view sky camera imagery with millimeter-wave cloud radar and ceilometer observations to produce 4D (three spatial dimensions plus time) estimates of cloud state and wind. The method operates in three stages: a cross-modal hierarchical aggregation module that combines image feature pyramids with instrument-derived vertical profiles through layer-wise cross-attention; a conditional variational refinement module that maps the resulting volume to physically consistent microphysical fields under differentiable radar and image forward models; and a correlation-based motion estimator that recovers per-voxel 3D wind vectors from consecutive volumetric reconstructions. On collocated observations from a semi-arid site, AtmoFuseNet reaches 0.026 g m^-3 liquid water content MAE and 1.18 m s^-1 wind speed MAE, improving over existing retrieval baselines. Ablation experiments isolate the contribution of each module.

</details>


### [2] [Streaming Gaussian Encoding for 4D Panoptic Occupancy Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30754)
*Maximilian Luz,Thomas Nürnberg,Yakov Miron,Abhinav Valada*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于流式高斯编码器的4D-POT方法，通过维护一个持久的体素场景表示，实现几何与语义上的时间一致性。该方法利用运动补偿和置信度引导的预算约束来传播高斯查询，并通过深度监督调节高斯不透明度作为可见性代理，从而实现置信度的时序累积。结合多帧训练策略，显著提升跟踪一致性，同时保持低计算开销，兼容现有基于掩码的流水线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于掩码的4D-POT方法在时间上频繁重新计算体素表示，导致几何时间一致性不足，尤其在遮挡和静态场景元素中表现不佳。需要一种能保持持久场景表示的方法以增强时间连贯性。

Method: 提出流式高斯编码器，将场景建模为固定大小的潜在高斯查询集，通过自车运动补偿进行传播，并在置信度引导下进行刷新；利用深度监督调节高斯不透明度作为可见性代理，实现置信度的时序聚合；采用温启动多帧训练策略。

Result: 在Occ3D-extended nuScenes和Waymo数据集上达到新的最佳性能，显著提升跟踪一致性，计算开销几乎不变，且可无缝集成到现有基于掩码的框架中。

Conclusion: 所提出的流式高斯编码器有效提升了相机基4D-POT的时间一致性，为长期、稳定、准确的场景理解提供了新范式。

Abstract: Camera-based 4D panoptic occupancy tracking (4D-POT) is a promising paradigm for holistic scene understanding from multi-view imagery, enabling joint reasoning about geometry, semantics, and object identities across time. Recent mask-based pipelines achieve strong performance by propagating instance queries across frames. However, their underlying volumetric representations are typically recomputed at each timestep, limiting geometric temporal consistency, particularly under occlusion and for static scene elements. To address this limitation, we propose a streaming Gaussian encoder that maintains a persistent volumetric scene representation for 4D-POT. Our method models the scene as a fixed-size set of latent Gaussian queries that are propagated via ego-motion compensation and refreshed under a confidence-guided budget constraint. Crucially, we shape Gaussian opacities through depth-based supervision to serve as proxy for visibility, enabling confidence to accumulate as a temporally aggregated measure of persistent scene support. Together with a warmup-based multi-frame training strategy, this yields representation-level temporal coherence beyond decoder-only tracking. Extensive experiments on Occ3D-extended nuScenes and Waymo establish a new state-of-the-art for camera-based 4D-POT, improving tracking consistency with negligible computational overhead while remaining fully compatible with existing mask-based pipelines. We provide code and models at https://sge.cs.uni-freiburg.de.

</details>


### [3] [Unveiling Transferability in Trajectory Prediction via Latent Scene Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30777)
*Theodor Westny,David Axelsson,Björn Olofsson,Erik Frisk*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一个框架，通过学习数据集的潜在表示并使用分布度量量化其相似性，以解决模型在不同数据集间泛化能力差的问题。研究覆盖24个主流数据集，发现迁移性得分与跨数据集模型性能高度相关，为数据集选择、预训练及大规模基础模型提供了实用指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有运动预测模型在不同数据集上表现不佳，主要由于场景布局、代理行为和感知条件的差异，亟需一种评估数据集相似性的方法以提升模型泛化能力。

Method: 提出一种基于潜在表示学习和分布度量的框架，用于量化多个轨迹数据集之间的相似性。

Result: 该框架生成的迁移性得分与跨数据集模型性能强相关，验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究为数据集选择、预训练策略和构建通用运动预测基础模型提供了有效工具，有助于实现更鲁棒、可泛化的预测系统。

Abstract: The growing availability of trajectory datasets has fueled major advances in data-driven motion prediction. Yet, models trained on one dataset often fail to generalize beyond their training domain as a result of differences in scene layouts, agent behaviors, and sensing conditions. A framework that learns latent representations of datasets and quantifies their similarity using distributional metrics is presented. This large-scale study covers 24 major datasets, including the most widely used motion-prediction benchmarks, and shows that the resulting transferability scores strongly correlate with cross-dataset model performance. The results provide practical guidance for dataset selection, pretraining, and large-scale foundation models for motion prediction, paving the way toward more generalizable and robust predictive systems.

</details>


### [4] [Simple Supervision Is Hard to Beat: A Bitter Lesson from Sparse Target Labels in Domain-Adaptive Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30795)
*Lijun Zhang,Ruinian Xu,Mudit Agrawal*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究在仅有少量目标域标注样本的情况下，如何提升源域训练的检测器在无标签目标域上的适应能力。提出一种简单有效的基线方法RTSM，通过引入少量标注数据构建监督损失，同时保持原有自训练框架不变，在多个设置下均显著提升性能（1.7到18.3 AP50），并验证了其他复杂反馈机制难以超越该基线，揭示了‘简单监督优于复杂设计’的核心结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在源域无监督域自适应目标检测中，尽管已有大量基于伪标签的自训练方法，但当目标域存在少量标注数据时，如何有效利用这些稀疏标注仍缺乏系统探索。现有方法多尝试复杂反馈机制，但效果有限且依赖具体模型。因此亟需一个简单、稳定且性能优越的基线方法来评估和指导未来研究。

Method: 提出Random-Target Supervised Mixing (RTSM)，将少量目标域标注样本用于构建监督检测损失，与原始无标签自训练分支并行运行，不改变原有架构。通过融合有监督信号与自训练信号，实现对目标域的有效适应。

Result: 在四种SFDA-OD方法、两种检测器、多种任务及1%至10%标签预算下，RTSM始终优于纯源域无监督适应，提升幅度达1.7至18.3 AP50。对比十种稀疏标注反馈插件（如伪标签筛选、物体补全、优化控制等），其增益有限且依赖模型，无法超越RTSM。

Conclusion: 在稀疏标注的源域无监督目标检测任务中，简单地引入少量标注监督已具备强大性能，远超复杂的反馈机制。因此，RTSM提供了一个简洁而高效的基准方法，应作为未来研究的锚点。

Abstract: Source-free domain adaptive object detection adapts a source-trained detector to an unlabeled target domain, typically through teacher-student self-training with pseudo-labels. We revisit this setting when a small, uniformly sampled subset of target images is labeled. We introduce Random-Target Supervised Mixing (RTSM), a simple anchor that incorporates these annotations through a supervised detection loss while leaving the original unlabeled adaptation branch unchanged. Across evaluations spanning four SFDA-OD methods, two object detectors, multiple adaptation tasks, and target-label budgets from 1% to 10%, RTSM consistently improves pure SFDA by 1.7 to 18.3 AP50. We then examine whether the same annotations can provide further gains by steering unlabeled self-training. To this end, we evaluate ten sparse-label feedback plugins covering pseudo-label selection, object completion, and optimization control, which yield limited and method-dependent gains over RTSM. These results reveal a bitter lesson for sparse-label SFDA-OD: simple supervision is hard to beat. RTSM therefore provides a simple yet effective anchor for sparse-label SFDA-OD.

</details>


### [5] [GaussLite: Online Task-Conditioned 3D Gaussian Splatting for Real-Time Robotic Mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30809)
*Annika Thomas,Mason Peterson,Jonathan P. How*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GaussLite 是一种任务驱动的 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) 映射系统，根据自然语言任务指令动态分配场景表示密度。它通过单次调用大语言模型（LLM）解析目标与锚定物体，并结合开放词汇检测器实现每帧的语义定位与像素级相关性掩码生成，从而在资源受限设备上以4 Hz实时运行。该方法在相同高斯点预算下，显著提升关键区域的重建质量（在Replica数据集上平均提升+2.72 dB，在真实硬件上提升+2.23 dB）。此外，可通过基于体素投票机制融合多个任务专用地图，仅共享7.08%的地图内容，性能优于拼接方式（+3.42 dB）


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3DGS系统对场景进行均匀表示，但许多下游机器人任务仅关注局部几何结构，导致计算资源浪费在无关区域，限制了在线处理能力或降低关键区域优化质量。因此需要一种能根据任务需求智能分配表示资源的方法

Method: GaussLite 利用一阶段大语言模型解析自然语言任务，提取目标与锚定对象；通过开放词汇检测器实现每帧的语义定位与分割，生成像素级相关性掩码；基于该掩码动态调节高斯点的生成密度、梯度传播与尺度，实现任务感知的资源分配；支持多任务地图的实时融合，采用体素级活跃优化计数投票机制

Result: 在相同高斯点预算和4 Hz实时映射条件下，GaussLite 在 Replica 数据集上的 ROI PSNR 平均提升 2.72 dB，真实硬件环境下提升 2.23 dB；多任务地图融合效果优于传统拼接，提升 3.42 dB，且仅需共享约 7.08% 的地图内容

Conclusion: GaussLite 成功实现了基于自然语言任务的自适应 3D 场景表示，有效提升了关键区域重建质量并优化了资源利用效率，为机器人任务导向的实时三维建图提供了高效解决方案

Abstract: Existing 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) systems distribute representation capacity uniformly across a scene, ignoring the fact that many downstream robotic tasks engage only a fraction of the reconstructed geometry. This causes valuable onboard compute to be allocated towards optimizing irrelevant parts of the scene, either limiting online capacity or under-optimizing the most relevant parts of the scene. We introduce GaussLite, a task-driven 3DGS mapping system that conditions its representation density on a natural-language task specification. Given a posed RGB-D stream and a task such as "prepare to pick up the object on the desk," GaussLite uses a one-shot LLM parser to extract target and anchor objects, which are grounded per-frame by an open-vocabulary detector and segmented to produce per-pixel relevance masks in real time. The mapper allocates seeding density, gradient flow and scaling by task relevance. At matched Gaussian budget and real-time mapping at 4 Hz on resource-constrained hardware, GaussLite outperforms baselines on ROI PSNR on the Replica Dataset by an average +2.72 dB and on a real-hardware demonstration in indoor and outdoor settings by +2.23 dB. We further show that two task-specialized agents' maps can be fused into a single shared map via per-voxel voting on active-optimization counts in real time, outperforming concatenation by +3.42 dB while only sharing an average 7.08% of the map.

</details>


### [6] [AVTok: 1D Unified Tokenization for Holistic Audio-Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30811)
*Kien T. Pham,I Chieh Chen,Qifeng Chen,Long Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: AVTok提出一种统一的音视频标记化方法，通过双流Transformer架构和共享编码器-解码器，将音视频对高效编码为统一的一维潜在表示，解决模态间表征差距与信息不平衡问题。采用分层训练策略提升重建能力，并在多种生成任务中表现优异，推动联合音视频建模发展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有音视频生成方法多采用双分支设计，存在表征差距和计算资源消耗大的问题，缺乏统一的音视频标记化机制，难以实现高质量的同步与语义对齐。

Method: 提出AVTok，基于双流Transformer架构，使用共享编码器-解码器和模态特定可学习查询，将音视频对编码为统一一维潜在表示，结合分层训练策略应对异构信息不平衡问题。

Result: AVTok在音视频重建及下游任务（如音频到视频、视频到音频、类别条件联合生成）中均表现出色，验证了其有效性与通用性。

Conclusion: AVTok为联合音视频标记化提供了新范式，有助于构建统一的大规模多模态音视频生成模型，具有重要应用前景。

Abstract: Audio-video generation has recently gained unprecedented research attention, aiming to synthesize high-quality sounding video content with fine-grained synchronization and semantic alignment between the auditory and visual components. The preceding methods predominantly adopt a dual-branch design with separate tokenization and generation modules per modality, neglecting the representation gap while necessitating intensive computational resources for proper training. Inspired by recent advancements in one-dimensional visual tokenization, we present \textbf{AVTok}, a novel unified tokenizer designated for holistic audio-video generation. AVTok features a dual-stream transformer-based architecture with shared encoder-decoder and modal-specific learnable queries to efficiently and effectively encode an audio-video pair into a compact one-dimensional latent representation with a unified codebook. To cope with the heterogeneous information imbalance that hinders AVTok from exploiting aligned audio-visual information, we devise a hierarchical training strategy to progressively realize reconstruction capabilities for each modality. Extensive experiments demonstrate that AVTok excels both in audio-video reconstruction and when integrated into downstream pipelines for audio-to-video, video-to-audio, and class-conditional joint audio-video generation. AVTok paves the way for the challenge of joint audio-video tokenization and provides a potential direction to build unified large multimodal models for audio-video generation.

</details>


### [7] [SyncCache: Exploiting Asymmetric Dynamics for Fast Audio-Driven Portrait Animation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30849)
*Juncheng Ma,Yuxuan Du,Yanan Sun,Zhening Xing,Changlin Li,Zhenyu Tang,Bo Li,Peng-Tao Jiang,Li Yuan,Daquan Zhou,Yonghong Tian*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SyncCache是一种针对基于DiT的肖像动画设计的免训练缓存加速方法，通过利用音频驱动动画中的空间和模态不对称性，显著提升推理速度。它通过空间非对称探测优先处理动态人脸区域的误差敏感性，并采用模态解耦缓存机制，重用稳定的块间残差，同时重新计算轻量级音频块以保持精确的口型同步。此外，引入缓存比率控制缓存容量，并将内存自适应缓存选择建模为离线动态规划问题，避免在线开销。实验表明，SyncCache在HunyuanVideo-Avatar和Wan-S2V上分别实现最高4.12倍和3.75倍加速，且视觉保真度近乎无损，音频对齐精准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有免训练扩散缓存方法主要针对文本条件生成，未考虑音频驱动肖像动画中的空间和模态不平衡问题，导致在实际应用中效率与精度难以兼顾。因此需要一种专门针对音频驱动肖像动画优化的缓存加速方法，以解决高计算成本与低延迟需求之间的矛盾。

Method: 提出SyncCache方法，包含：1）空间非对称探测（Spatially-Asymmetric Probing），聚焦于动态人脸区域的误差敏感性；2）模态解耦缓存（Modality-Decoupled Caching），通过重用稳定块间残差绕过复杂DiT块，仅重新计算轻量级音频块；3）引入缓存比率控制缓存容量，并将缓存选择建模为离线动态规划问题，实现内存自适应且无在线开销。

Result: 在HunyuanVideo-Avatar和Wan-S2V数据集上，SyncCache分别实现了最高4.12倍和3.75倍的推理加速，同时保持近似无损的视觉质量与精确的音频对齐，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: SyncCache通过显式建模音频驱动肖像动画中的空间与模态不对称性，有效解决了高计算成本带来的推理延迟问题，在保证高质量输出的同时实现了显著加速，为高效音频驱动动画提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Diffusion Transformers (DiTs) have significantly advanced audio-driven portrait animation, but their high computational cost leads to substantial inference latency. Although training-free diffusion caching accelerates inference significant, existing methods are primarily developed for text-conditioned generation and overlook the spatial and modality imbalances inherent in audio-driven portrait animation. In this paper, we propose SyncCache, a training-free caching acceleration method tailored for DiT-based portrait animation that explicitly exploits asymmetric dynamics. Specifically, high-frequency dynamics driven by audio conditions and concentrated in human regions are more challenging and critical to cache and reuse than the low-frequency visual background in portrait animation. First, we introduce Spatially-Asymmetric Probing to prioritize error sensitivity in dynamic human region. Second, through Modality-Decoupled Caching, we bypass heavy DiT block by reusing stable inter-block residuals, while continuously recomputing lightweight audio blocks to preserve precise lip synchronization. Furthermore, we introduce a cache ratio to control cache capacity and formulate memory-adaptive cache selection as an offline dynamic programming problem without online overhead. Extensive experiments demonstrate that SyncCache achieves superior speed-quality trade-offs, delivering up to 4.12x acceleration on HunyuanVideo-Avatar and 3.75x on Wan-S2V with near-lossless visual fidelity and precise audio alignment.

</details>


### [8] [The Label Imitation Game: Turing Test Network for Zero-Shot Pseudo-Label Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30875)
*Brent A. Griffin,Jason J. Corso*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出基于图灵测试思想的标签模仿游戏（LIG）框架，通过训练一个任务无关的“裁判”网络（TTN）来评估伪标签，以克服基础模型伪标签中的幻觉问题。该方法在多个数据集上显著提升三类先进视觉-语言模型的标签准确率，无需额外标注或重新训练，且具备零样本任务迁移能力，可有效处理复杂目标检测任务。实验显示，其在最差类别上带来28%的F1分数提升，结合微调可达44%；同时发现“类别复兴”现象，使下游模型恢复对易受迁移影响类别的识别能力。代码与预训练模型已开源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于零样本推理的伪标签方法虽能实现大规模标注，但受限于模型幻觉导致的错误标签，传统阈值过滤难以有效解决。需要一种更智能、上下文感知的机制来精准剔除错误标签，提升伪标签质量。

Method: 设计并训练一个任务无关的图灵测试网络（TTN），作为伪标签的“裁判”，通过对抗式质询方式评估候选标签的合理性。利用多数据集上下文信息进行训练，使TTN学习到鲁棒的语义-上下文逻辑，从而在无监督条件下完成伪标签筛选。

Result: 在四个不同数据集上的实验表明，TTN能显著提高三种主流视觉-语言模型的伪标签准确性，不依赖人工标注或重训练；即使仅在图像分类数据上训练的TTN，也能成功用于目标检测伪标签的净化，实现28%至44%的F1得分提升；还观察到‘类别复兴’现象，即被污染的类别信号得以恢复，召回率从零回升。

Conclusion: 提出的标签模仿游戏（LIG）框架及对应的图灵测试网络（TTN）为伪标签生成提供了一种高效、通用且零样本迁移能力强的新范式，能够有效抑制幻觉，提升下游模型性能，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: Foundation model pseudo-labeling - labeling data strictly via zero-shot inference - enables massive scale, but performance is undermined by hallucinations that evade standard thresholds. To eliminate these errors, we introduce the Turing-inspired Label Imitation Game (LIG), a framework that formalizes pseudo-label pruning as an adversarial interrogation. Rather than filtering labels via isolated thresholds, we use the LIG to train a Turing Test Network (TTN), a task-agnostic "judge" that evaluates candidate pseudo-labels within a dataset-wide context. Experiments across four diverse datasets demonstrate the TTN's robustness, consistently enhancing label accuracy for three state-of-the-art vision-language models without costly supervision or retraining. Crucially, we demonstrate that learned semantic-contextual logic is a robust alternative to spatial-geometric verification, enabling a unique zero-shot task transfer capability - a TTN trained strictly on image classification datasets can effectively prune complex object detection pseudo-labels. This pruning yields F1-score gains of 28% for the worst-performing baseline categories and 44% with task-specific fine-tuning. Significantly, we also observe Category Revival, where the TTN pruning "detoxifies" the training signal for downstream models and enables them to recover from zero recall on transfer-vulnerable classes. The pre-trained TTN models and code are available at https://github.com/voxel51/ttn.

</details>

Abstract: In the verification of in-vehicle cameras, simulation technology using virtual spaces has advanced, enabling pre-evaluation of false detections and missed detections in various scenarios. For traffic signs installed at high altitudes, distance measurement using LiDAR or stereo cameras is difficult, requiring size estimation from monocular images. This paper proposes a method for estimating the scale of an object by decomposing it into multiple structural elements and integrating external knowledge regarding design rules, geometric relationships, and conventional dimensions. Specifically, this method detects each component from a monocular image and estimates the size of each component by considering its structural relationships and dimensional consistency with surrounding elements. Furthermore, it generates a 3D asset of the object by reconstructing the estimated components. This method makes it possible to place 3D assets with a scale approximating the real environment within a digital twin space and is expected to contribute to improving the verification accuracy of in-vehicle cameras for autonomous driving in virtual environments.

### [10] [GRAPE: Graph-Augmented Prototype Explanations for Interactive Medical Image Diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30901)
*Rasul Khanbayov,Hasan Kurban*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GRAPE 是一种统一的原型医学图像分类架构，解决了现有方法在临床应用中的三大局限：独立处理病灶、放大不安全医生反馈、新增病灶需全量重训练。通过图注意力任务头建模解剖概念共现，提升宏平均F1得分13.8个百分点；引入概念不匹配安全检查机制，有效识别85%错误标注，且无额外推理开销；采用开放词汇原型锚定，仅需单个标注图像即可添加新病灶，无需修改其他组件。实验显示在NIH ChestX-ray14和TBX11K数据集上显著提升定位精度，三类能力仅增加1~2毫秒延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有原型医学图像分类器存在三个关键临床局限：将病灶视为独立、对不安全医生反馈敏感、新增病灶需重新训练。这些限制阻碍了其在真实医疗场景中的部署与扩展。

Method: 提出GRAPE框架，包含三个核心组件：(1) 图注意力任务头，用于建模解剖概念之间的共现关系；(2) 概念不匹配安全检查机制，检测模型预测与医生标注之间的矛盾；(3) 开放词汇原型锚定，通过文本-视觉对齐实现新病灶的快速添加。

Result: 在TBX11K数据集上，宏平均F1提升13.8个百分点；概念不匹配检测准确率达85%，远超MC-Dropout的51%；在NIH ChestX-ray14上，仅用一个胸腔积液样本即恢复全监督定位性能；在病变定位方面，原型图比端到端基线提升2.6倍。三项功能仅增加1~2毫秒延迟，适合实时应用。

Conclusion: GRAPE成功构建了一个可解释、安全、可扩展的原型医学图像分类系统，为临床部署提供了实用解决方案，并已在GitHub开源。

Abstract: Prototype-based medical image classifiers present three clinical limitations: they treat findings as independent, silently amplify unsafe physician feedback, and require full retraining whenever a new finding is needed. We present GRAPE (Graph-Augmented Prototype Explanations), a unified architecture that addresses all three challenges. First, a Graph Attention Task Head models anatomical concept co-occurrence, boosting macro-F1 by +13.8,pp over the prototype baseline on TBX11K. Second, a Concept-Mismatch Safety Check - the first such mechanism in prototype-based medical classifiers - warns when the model's dominant finding inside a doctor-drawn region conflicts with the claimed label, catching 85% of erroneous annotations versus 51% for MC-Dropout with no extra inference cost. Third, Open-Vocabulary Prototype Anchoring aligns visual prototypes to clinical text, allowing a new finding to be added from a single labeled image without modifying any other component. On NIH ChestX-ray14, one Effusion example recovers full-supervision localization accuracy; on TBX11K, prototype maps achieve 2.6x better lesion localization than end-to-end baselines. All three capabilities add only +1~ms latency at interactive batch size. The project page is https://github.com/KurbanIntelligenceLab/GRAPE.

### [11] [No Adaptation Without Observation: Observability-Constrained Test-Time Prompt Tuning for LiDAR Semantic Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30937)
*Linlian Jiang,Wentao Ju,Sadman Rakib Pinon,Jianwei Xian,Zhixiang Chi,Xinxin Zuo,Yang Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种几何约束的测试时提示调优框架：利用深度一致性光束终止与邻域支持估计感知可靠性；基于可靠性重加权空间监督；仅更新轻量级提示适配器；通过空间门控防止不可靠区域干扰；采用时间平滑的原型对齐策略累积可靠语义信息以稳定更新。

Result: 在标准LiDAR基准测试上，该方法在无额外标注的前提下，有效提升了模型在部署环境变化下的适应稳定性与分割精度，验证了其有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该方法通过几何约束与时空协同的自适应机制，实现了对LiDAR语义分割在动态环境中的高效、稳定适应，为实际部署提供了可行方案。

Abstract: LiDAR semantic segmentation often degrades under real-world deployment due to evolving sensing conditions, while collecting new annotations for retraining is impractical. Test-time adaptation (TTA) updates model parameters online using pseudo-label supervision, but directly applying standard TTA strategies to LiDAR data is challenging. Because pseudo-label reliability is spatially heteroscedastic under range-dependent sparsity and occlusion, uniform updates on globally shared parameters can inject unstable gradients and destabilize adaptation. We propose a geometry-constrained test-time prompt tuning framework for LiDAR semantic segmentation. Our method estimates per-location sensing reliability from depth-consistent beam terminations and neighborhood support, and uses it to reweight spatial supervision. Adaptation is confined to lightweight prompt adapters inserted into a frozen backbone, with spatial gating to prevent unreliable regions from perturbing globally shared representations. A temporally smoothed prototype alignment strategy further stabilizes online updates by accumulating reliable semantic evidence over time. Experiments on standard LiDAR benchmarks demonstrate improved adaptation stability and segmentation performance under deployment variations without additional annotations.

### [12] [Learning Where to Look: A Reinforcement Learning Framework for Robust Micro-Ultrasound Prostate Cancer Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30951)
*Mohammad Mahdi Abootorabi,Sina Namazi,Armin Saadat,Lyuyang Wang,Obed Dzikunu,Paul F. R. Wilson,Zhuoxin Guo,Brian Wodlinger,Parvin Mousavi,Purang Abolmaesumi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Prost-RL 是一种基于强化学习的空间感知推理框架，用于提升微超声（μUS）在前列腺癌检测中的准确性。该方法通过轻量级强化学习策略生成可解释的注意力图，作为软提示指导图像级分类和癌症风险热图预测，并结合自适应策略优化（APO）与噪声鲁棒损失函数以应对弱标签噪声和类别不平衡问题，在多中心数据集上实现了79.0±3.5 AUROC的核心水平检测性能，显著优于现有基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前微超声在前列腺癌检测中依赖医生经验，存在显著的观察者间差异；尽管机器学习可降低这种变异性，但受限于稀疏且嘈杂的标注（如仅核心级别的病理结果，缺乏像素级病变标注），训练可靠深度模型极具挑战性。因此亟需一种能有效利用弱监督信息、同时具备可解释性的智能辅助诊断方法。

Method: 提出 Prost-RL 框架，将 μUS 中的前列腺癌检测建模为一个空间感知的、策略驱动的推理任务。该框架融合轻量级强化学习策略与基础模型编码器-解码器结构，通过策略学习‘关注何处’，生成可解释的空间注意力图，用作软提示以指导癌症概率热图预测和图像级分类。引入自适应策略优化（APO）稳定混合监督-强化学习训练过程，并设计结合对称交叉熵与负熵正则化的噪声鲁棒目标函数，缓解弱标签噪声并促进精确定位。

Result: 在包含6,607个活检核心、来自693名患者及五个临床中心的数据集上，Prost-RL 在核心级别检测中达到 79.0±3.5 AUROC，80% 特异性下敏感度为 64.6±6.3%，较最强基线提升2.1 AUROC和4.5个百分点敏感度；在临床显著性癌症分类中取得 79.3±5.8 AUROC。所学策略能有效聚焦于与活检区域对齐的解剖位置，提供透明、空间明确的判别依据。

Conclusion: Prost-RL 成功将弱监督下的前列腺癌检测转化为可解释的策略驱动推理任务，显著提升了检测性能并增强了模型透明度，为微超声在临床中的智能化应用提供了有力支持。代码已开源，便于复现与推广。

Abstract: Micro-ultrasound ($μ$US) is a new, emerging, and promising imaging modality for prostate cancer (PCa) detection, but accurate identification of suspicious tissue remains highly dependent on clinical experience, leading to substantial inter-observer variability. Machine-learning assistance can reduce this variability; however, training reliable deep models is challenging because supervision is sparse and noisy -- typically limited to core-level histopathology outcomes (e.g., cancer grade and its percentage in a biopsy core) without pixel-level lesion annotations and under severe class imbalance. We introduce Prost-RL, which reframes $μ$US PCa detection as a spatially aware, policy-driven inference problem by learning where to look before decoding. Prost-RL integrates a lightweight reinforcement-learning policy into a foundation-model encoder-decoder to generate interpretable spatial attention maps that act as soft prompts for both cancer-likelihood heatmap prediction and image-level classification. We further propose Adaptive Policy Optimization (APO) to stabilize hybrid supervised-RL training and a noise-robust objective combining symmetric cross-entropy with negative-entropy regularization to mitigate weak-label noise and encourage sharp localization. On a cohort of 6,607 biopsy cores from 693 patients across five clinical sites, Prost-RL achieves $79.0\pm3.5$ AUROC with $64.6\pm6.3$% sensitivity at 80% specificity for core-level detection (+2.1 AUROC and +4.5 sensitivity points over the strongest baseline), and $79.3\pm5.8$ AUROC for clinically significant cancer classification. The learned policy highlights biopsy-aligned regions, providing transparent, spatially grounded evidence alongside quantitative risk predictions. Code is available at: https://github.com/DeepRCL/Prost-RL.

### [13] [PhotoQuilt: Training-Free Arbitrary-Resolution Photomosaics via Bootstrapped Tiled Denoising](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30968)
*Koorosh Roohi,Javad Rajabi,Andrew Fleet,Babak Taati*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PhotoQuilt是一种无需训练的框架，可生成任意分辨率的高质量照片马赛克。它通过分步式去噪过程，在保持全局结构的同时增强局部细节，克服了扩散模型在高分辨率生成中难以兼顾整体与局部的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在生成高分辨率照片马赛克时面临计算成本高、局部细节与全局结构难以兼顾的挑战。直接高分辨率生成易导致图像平滑化，而基于补丁的拼接方式则丢失整体布局。因此需要一种高效且能同时保证局部真实感和全局一致性的新方法。

Method: PhotoQuilt采用自举式分块去噪策略：先在低分辨率下生成全局布局以确定结构，再在潜在空间中上采样并重新注入噪声，使每个固定区域独立进行去噪，从而在保持整体一致性的同时实现每个瓷砖的高质量生成。

Result: 实验表明，PhotoQuilt在全局结构一致性和局部细节真实性方面均优于现有基线方法，且在大规模画布上具有良好的扩展性，避免了二次注意力开销。

Conclusion: PhotoQuilt提供了一种高效、可扩展的高分辨率照片马赛克生成方案，通过分离局部生成与全局布局，有效解决了传统扩散模型在多尺度生成中的瓶颈问题。

Abstract: Photomosaics are large images whose local regions are seen as independent tiles while their overall arrangement forms a coherent scene. Generating them at high resolution, with every tile convincing in its own right, is computationally expensive, since the canvas must hold many detailed tiles at once. We present PhotoQuilt, a training-free framework that generates photomosaics at arbitrary resolution. Diffusion models struggle to satisfy both scales at once, as direct high-resolution generation is costly and tends toward one smooth image rather than a mosaic, while patch-based tiling keeps local detail but loses global structure. PhotoQuilt resolves this with a bootstrapped tiled denoising procedure. We first produce a global composition at low resolution to fix the layout, then upscale it in latent space and re-inject noise to restore generative capacity. Denoising proceeds within fixed tiles, so each forms its own image while the shared global structure holds them in one layout. Because tile generation is handled separately, PhotoQuilt scales to large canvases without quadratic attention cost. Experiments show that PhotoQuilt outperforms current baselines on both global structure and local realism.

</details>


### [14] [Auditing Generalization in AI-Generated Video Detection: A Six-Control Protocol and the VidAudit Toolkit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31004)
*Mert Onur Cakiroglu,Zhihe Lu,Mehmet Dalkilic,Hasan Kurban*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了当前AI生成视频检测基准（如GenVidBench和AIGVDBench）中存在的未控制混淆因素，可能导致性能评估虚高。通过构建一个经过审计的综合评估协议，整合六项标准控制措施，重新评估六个代表性特征源（包括三个已发表检测器和三个重构信号源），发现此前表现优异的模型在严格测试下性能大幅下降，甚至接近随机水平。研究提出应以多维度指标（AUC、阈值裕度、操作点召回率、校准性）取代单一数值评价，并引入白盒正向控制TemporalSpec（基于编码器运动矢量），通过跨底物特征融合（XSFF）实现真实互补性。最终发布VidAudit工具包，包含14个经统一审计的检测器、统一API、排行榜与元数据，推动评估从排名导向转向对测量有效性的真实检验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI生成视频检测基准存在未控制的混淆因素，导致评估结果可能夸大模型的真实泛化能力，亟需建立更严谨、可审计的评估协议以确保评估结果的有效性和可信度。

Method: 构建并应用一套整合六项标准控制措施的审计协议，对多个检测器进行跨数据集复现测试；引入白盒正向控制TemporalSpec，结合跨底物特征融合（XSFF）验证互补性；开发VidAudit工具包，实现统一评估与公开共享。

Result: 三特征剪辑长度分类器在未审计条件下达到0.998 LOGO AUC，但在审计后降至0.529（接近随机）；CLIP基线暴露携带数据集身份的问题；2025年检测器WaveRep在跨分布测试中仍保持0.996 AUC且真实-真实一致性处于随机水平；多个高AUC方法在部署级误报率（FPR=0.1%）下召回率跌至个位数，排行榜顺序发生改变。

Conclusion: 当前评估体系需从单一指标排名转向多维审计框架，强调测量有效性而非表面性能；建议采用包含AUC、阈值裕度、操作点召回率和校准性的审计组合指标；通过VidAudit工具包推动检测评估向透明、可验证方向发展。

Abstract: AI-generated video detection benchmarks such as GenVidBench and AIGVDBench are the de facto leaderboards, yet most evaluation protocols leave uncontrolled confounds that can inflate reported generalization. As an existence proof, a three-feature clip-length classifier reaches a leave-one-generator-out (LOGO) AUC of 0.998 on GenVidBench under unaudited evaluation, while measuring nothing about motion. A 20-paper survey finds none applying all six standard controls that would catch this, so we combine them into an audited protocol and apply it to six representative feature sources (three published detectors and three repurposed signal sources), re-running it cross-dataset on AIGVDBench. The audit both debunks and certifies: the trivial classifier collapses to near chance (0.529), a CLIP baseline is caught carrying dataset identity, and the 2025 forensic detector WaveRep clears the floor at out-of-distribution LOGO AUC 0.996 with chance-level real-vs-real coherence. At a deployable FPR of 0.1%, multiple high-AUC methods fall to single-digit recall and the leaderboard order changes, so we recommend an audited tuple (AUC, above-floor margin, operating-point recall, and calibration) over a single number. As a white-box positive control, we add TemporalSpec (codec motion vectors); via cross-substrate feature fusion (XSFF), a second substrate adds genuine complementarity that survives the audit. We release VidAudit, to our knowledge the largest unified and audited detector collection for this task, providing 14 detectors behind one plugin API, a leaderboard, and Croissant metadata, available at https://github.com/KurbanIntelligenceLab/vidaudit. Together, the protocol and toolkit move evaluation from leaderboard rank toward whether a result measures what it claims.

### [15] [Dense Structural Priors for Sparse Functional Landmark Localization in Surgical Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31007)
*Chenyan Jing,Hao Ding,Lalithkumar Seenivasan,Jacob M. Delgado López,Mathias Unberath*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于视觉基础模型（如SAM 3）的稀疏动作感知关键点定位，提出一种轻量级优化框架，利用零样本、点提示的结构掩码提供密集器械级上下文，避免手动像素级标注。通过多帧粗略网络预测工具尖端和锚点提示，结合视觉与热力图特征融合，实现功能关键点的精细化预测。对比了直接掩码增强监督、预测生成掩码先验优化和辅助掩码监督三种方式，发现后两者能有效引导动作相关的关键点定位。在多个外科视频数据集上验证，无需人工标注即可达到尖端定位F1 72.4%、锚点58.0%，证明了该方法在异构条件下的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉基础模型虽可跨多样手术视频提供可迁移的对象级结构，但其分割输出缺乏动作相关语义，无法准确表达功能性手术地标。传统方法难以区分工具范围与具体操作相关的关键点（如夹持、抓取、分离等），因此亟需一种无需像素级标注、能捕捉动作依赖性的关键点定位方法。

Method: 采用SAM 3作为结构先验，构建轻量级细化框架；通过多帧粗略网络预测尖端与锚点提示，生成非真值掩码，并与视觉特征及热力图特征融合，进行功能关键点的精细化预测；比较三种掩码引入策略：直接掩码增强监督、预测生成掩码先验、辅助掩码监督，以探索如何最优地融入基础模型提供的结构信息。

Result: 在包含60个手术视频共7,867个片段的数据集上，无需人工像素级标注，模型在尖端定位上达到72.4% F1，在锚点定位上达到58.0% F1。直接使用掩码作为监督会偏向于宽泛工具区域的学习，而预测生成的掩码先验和辅助监督则提供了有效的中间结构指导，显著提升动作相关关键点的定位精度。

Conclusion: 本研究验证了将视觉基础模型作为结构先验在动作感知关键点定位中的有效性。通过轻量级框架与合理掩码引入策略，可在不依赖人工标注的前提下，实现高精度、动作敏感的手术器械关键点定位，为智能手术系统提供可靠的技术支持。

Abstract: Vision foundation models such as SAM 3 can provide transferable object-level structure across diverse surgical video conditions, but segmentation outputs do not explicitly encode the action-conditioned semantics that define functional surgical landmarks. Estimating instrument extent and geometry differs from localizing the tip or anchor relevant to clipping, grasping, or dissecting. We investigate vision foundation model-enabled sparse action-aware landmark localization, using zero-shot, point-prompted structural masks to provide dense instrument-level context without manual pixel-level mask annotations. We propose a lightweight refinement framework that uses SAM 3 as a structural prior. A coarse multi-frame network predicts tip and anchor prompts, generating non-oracle masks that are fused with visual and heatmap features to refine functional landmark predictions. We compare direct mask-augmented supervision, prediction-derived mask-prior refinement, and auxiliary mask supervision to examine how vision foundation model-derived structure should enter a precision-oriented localization system. Experiments on 7,867 clips from 60 surgical videos spanning YouTube, Cholec80, HeiChole, SurgVU, and CRCD evaluate the approach under heterogeneous conditions. Without manual pixel-level mask annotations for training, the proposed model achieves overall F1 scores of 72.4% for tip and 58.0% for anchor localization. Directly imposing masks on heatmap targets biases learning toward broad tool regions, whereas prediction-derived priors and auxiliary supervision provide effective intermediate structural guidance for action-dependent landmark prediction.

</details>


### [16] [Dual Sparse Aggregation Transformer for Multispectral Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31015)
*Wencong Wu,Xiuwei Zhang,Hanlin Yin,Hongxi Zhang,Yanning Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种新型的双稀疏聚合Transformer（DSAFormer），用于多光谱目标检测。该方法通过引入空间和通道级别的稀疏交叉注意力机制，有效减少无关区域的信息交互，提升跨模态互补信息的利用效率。同时，设计了多尺度特征精炼层与可学习加权融合块，以增强特征表达并实现高效的多模态融合。在四个公开数据集上验证了其优越性，性能优于现有先进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer的多光谱目标检测方法通常使用所有可用令牌进行相似性计算，导致来自无关区域的冗余信息交互，从而降低检测性能。因此，亟需一种能够有效筛选关键信息、抑制冗余交互的新方法。

Method: 提出DSAFormer，包含双稀疏Transformer（DSFormer）和可学习加权融合块（LAFB）。DSFormer采用空间稀疏多头交叉注意力（SSMHCA）和通道稀疏多头交叉注意力（CSMHCA）机制，在空间和通道层面仅保留高相似度的查询-键匹配，减少无效交互；引入多尺度特征精炼层（MSFRL）聚合层次化特征并抑制冗余信息。LAFB通过特征重加权实现模内与模间特征的有效融合。

Result: 在MFAD、FLIR、M$^3$FD和LLVIP四个公开数据集上，DSAFormer均取得了优于当前主流方法的检测性能，证明了其有效性与鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 所提出的DSAFormer通过双稀疏机制和可学习融合策略，显著提升了多光谱目标检测中跨模态信息的利用效率，为多模态视觉任务提供了一种高效、精准的新范式。

Abstract: Transformer-based approaches have obtained excellent performance in multispectral object detection tasks due to their ability to model long-range dependencies and capture complementary information. However, previous transformer-based multispectral detection methods tend to use all available tokens for similarity calculation, which results in redundant information interaction from irrelevant areas, leading to degraded detection performance. To overcome this challenge, we propose a novel Dual Sparse Aggregation Transformer (DSAFormer) for multispectral object detection, which consists of a Dual Sparse Transformer (DSFormer) and a Learnable Addition Fusion Block (LAFB). Specifically, the DSFormer is designed to exploit and boost cross-modal complementary information, thereby improving detection performance. It incorporates three key components: A Spatial Sparse Multi-Head Cross-Attention (SSMHCA) mechanism selectively captures cross-modal relationships at the spatial level by reserving only the high query-key similarity scores, eliminating irrelevant interactions. A Channel Sparse Multi-Head Cross-Attention (CSMHCA) mechanism performs similar sparse calculations at the channel level to enhance feature representation and filter out low matching query-key. A Multi-Scale Feature Refinement Layer (MSFRL) is developed to aggregate hierarchical features and suppress redundant information. To effectively fuse multimodal features, the LAFB is introduced to aggregate intramodal and intermodal feature information by feature reweighting. Extensive experimental results have demonstrated that our proposed DSAFormer achieves better detection performance against state-of-the-art methods on four public datasets, including the MFAD, FLIR, M$^3$FD, and LLVIP. The source code of our DSAFormer will be released at https://github.com/WenCongWu/DSAFormer.

</details>


### [17] [WarpI2I: Image Warping for Image-to-Image Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31018)
*Shen Zheng,Anurag Ghosh,Gaurav Parmar,Srinivasa Narasimhan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于显著性引导的 warp-unwarp 框架，通过在编码前将空间表示重新分配到显著区域，提升潜在扩散模型在图像到图像翻译任务中对细节结构的保留能力。该方法无需修改模型架构，计算开销极小，并可扩展至视频处理。此外，还设计了基于外绘的合成数据生成流程，以提升图像重光照等任务的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有潜在扩散模型在进行图像到图像翻译时，由于编码器将高分辨率输入压缩到空间下采样的潜在空间，导致细粒度结构难以保留。为解决此问题，需在不增加潜在分辨率的前提下增强结构保真度。

Method: 提出一种基于显著性的 warp-unwarp 框架：先根据显著图对输入图像进行空间扭曲，使关键区域获得更多表示容量；随后使用原扩散模型处理扭曲后的图像；最后通过逆向扭曲恢复原始结构。同时引入基于外绘的合成数据生成方法，用于构建高质量配对数据集。

Result: 在人物重光照、驾驶场景重光照与转换任务中，均实现了更好的结构保留、光照忠实度和图像质量。框架具备良好的时间稳定性，适用于视频任务，且无需额外架构改动或显著计算开销。

Conclusion: 所提方法是一种高效、通用且轻量级的解决方案，有效提升了潜伏扩散模型在图像到图像翻译中的细节保持能力，尤其适用于需要高精度结构保留的应用场景。

Abstract: Image-to-image (I2I) translation has achieved strong results in tasks like human relighting and driving scene translation using latent diffusion models (LDMs). However, compact LDMs often struggle to preserve fine-grained structures because the encoder compresses high-resolution inputs into a spatially downsampled latent space. To address this issue, we propose a simple saliency-guided warp-unwarp framework that reallocates spatial representation toward salient regions before encoding, enabling better preservation of structural details without increasing latent resolution. The warped image is processed by the original diffusion model and then mapped back via an inverse warp. In addition, we propose a simple and efficient outpainting-based synthetic data generation pipeline to produce high-quality paired data for image relighting. Our method is model-agnostic, requires no architectural modification, and introduces negligible computational overhead. Experiments on human relighting, driving scene relighting, and translation demonstrate improved structural preservation, lighting faithfulness, and image quality, with our framework extending naturally to video via frame-by-frame application with good temporal stability. Project Webpage: https://shenzheng2000.github.io/WarpI2I.github.io

</details>


### [18] [TerraDiT-$Ω$: Unified Spatial Control for Satellite Image Synthesis with Any Geospatial Primitive](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31029)
*Brian Wei,Srikumar Sastry,Daniel Cher,Eric Xing,Nathan Jacobs*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TerraDiT-$Ω$ 是一种统一的空间控制框架，能够直接从任何原生地理空间矢量数据（如多边形、折线、边界框、点）生成卫星图像。该方法通过几何感知局部注意力机制，将显式的几何信息注入注意力空间，支持在不同标注成本下的可控布局生成，适用于城市规划等设计任务，并与端到端地理人工智能工作流兼容。实验表明，其在多种条件格式下均优于密集和稀疏控制基线，且可实现可控的合成数据增强，提升土地覆盖分割、目标检测、道路图提取和场景分类等下游任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卫星影像具有复杂的空间结构和语义差异，传统基于自然图像的方法在处理时面临标注成本高或保真度低的问题，且难以与地理信息中常用的矢量原语兼容。因此需要一种能直接利用原生地理空间矢量数据生成高质量卫星图像的新方法。

Method: 提出Geometry-Aware Local Attention机制，将精确（多边形、折线）与粗略（边界框、点）的地理矢量作为条件输入，联合建模几何特征以指导图像生成；采用统一框架支持多种标注形式，实现灵活可控的生成。

Result: 在所有条件格式下，TerraDiT-$Ω$ 均显著优于现有密集控制与稀疏控制基线；通过单一模型实现可控合成数据增强，有效提升多个下游任务的性能。

Conclusion: TerraDiT-$Ω$ 实现了对地理空间矢量原语的直接生成支持，兼具灵活性、高效性与兼容性，为地理空间生成建模提供了新范式，推动了面向城市规划等应用的可控合成数据生成与端到端GeoAI发展。

Abstract: Generative models have achieved remarkable progress, yet applying them to satellite imagery remains challenging. Unlike natural imagery, satellite scenes are structured by spatially complex and semantically distinct geometries. Prior work addresses this complexity by adapting natural image frameworks using dense rasters or sparse prompts, trading off annotation cost and fidelity while breaking compatibility with vector primitives commonly used to represent geographic information. We introduce TerraDiT-$Ω$, a unified spatial control framework that generates satellite imagery directly from any native geospatial primitive. By jointly leveraging precise annotations (polygons, polylines) and coarser ones (bounding boxes, points), the model supports controllable layouts across varying annotation budgets, broadening applicability to design tasks such as urban planning while remaining naturally compatible with end-to-end GeoAI workflows. To effectively leverage these primitives during generation, we propose Geometry-Aware Local Attention, a conditioning mechanism that injects explicit geometric cues into the attention space. Across all conditioning formats, our approach consistently outperforms both dense-control and sparse-control baselines. Furthermore, this flexibility enables controllable synthetic data augmentation using a single generative model, improving downstream performance on land-cover segmentation, object detection, road graph extraction, and scene classification. Code, data, and weights are available at https://github.com/mvrl/TerraDiT.

</details>


### [19] [Learning Video Dynamics with Predictive Differentiable Rendering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31050)
*Yujin Tang,Tian Zhou,Xin Lin,Cheng Tan,Yifan Hu,Rong Jin,SouYoung Jin,Liang Sun*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为PDR的新型端到端视频预测范式，通过结合2D高斯表示的轻量级适配器PredGS和CUDA加速的可微分渲染器predgsplat，有效提升了视频预测中的空间细节保留与视觉保真度。该方法克服了传统像素级均方误差（MSE）导致的模糊问题，采用L1与SSIM联合损失优化，在多个真实世界基准测试中显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有确定性视频预测模型在离散像素空间中运行，依赖像素级均方误差（MSE）优化，常导致预测结果过平滑、缺乏细粒度视觉细节，无法准确捕捉连续视觉世界的动态变化。

Method: 提出Predictive Differentiable Rendering（PDR）框架，引入基于2D高斯表示的轻量级适配器PredGS，无缝集成于现有像素空间预测器；开发CUDA加速的可微分2D高斯渲染器predgsplat，支持任意通道，每个高斯具有5 + C个可学习参数（位置、尺度、旋转及C个通道幅值），实现高达10倍的渲染速度提升；使用L1与SSIM联合损失进行优化，减少MSE带来的模糊倾向。

Result: 在TaxiBJ、WeatherBench、KTH和Human3.6M等多个真实世界基准上，PDR持续超越现有方法，在细节保留、视觉保真度和预测准确性方面表现卓越。

Conclusion: PDR通过连接离散与连续表示，实现了高质量、高保真度的视频预测，为未来视觉世界建模提供了新的有效范式。

Abstract: How to accurately predict a high-fidelity future world? While the visual world is inherently continuous, existing deterministic video prediction models operate in discrete pixel space and are mainly optimized with pixel-wise mean squared error (MSE), which often leads to over-smoothed predictions and a lack of fine-grained visual details. To address these limitations, we propose Predictive Differentiable Rendering (PDR), a novel end-to-end video prediction paradigm that bridges the gap between discrete and continuous representations. Inspired by recent progress in 3D reconstruction with 3D Gaussian Splatting, we introduce PredGS, a lightweight and plug-and-play adapter based on 2D Gaussian representation, which could be seamlessly integrated with existing pixel space predictors, significantly improving spatial detail preservation with negligible computational overhead. Furthermore, we develop predgsplat, a CUDA-accelerated differentiable 2D Gaussian renderer supporting arbitrary channels. Each Gaussian is defined by 5 + C learnable parameters (position, scale, rotation, and C channel amplitudes) and achieves up to 10x faster rendering than the baseline. Optimized by a combined L1 and SSIM loss, PDR overcomes the inherent blurring tendencies of MSE Loss, significantly enhancing the prediction performance. Extensive experiments on diverse real-world benchmarks, including TaxiBJ, WeatherBench, KTH, and Human3.6M, demonstrate that PDR consistently surpasses existing methods, delivering superior detail preservation, visual fidelity, and predictive accuracy.

</details>


### [20] [ADAPT: Attention Dynamics Alignment with Preference Tuning for Faithful MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31054)
*Zhiyuan Yao,Zheren Fu,Zhixiao Zheng,Jiajun Li,Yi Tu,Zhendong Mao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出ADAPT框架，通过干预文本到图像的交叉注意力动态来缓解多模态大模型中的幻觉问题。该框架包含三个核心组件：基于早期解码阶段的视觉锚点以提供稳定的空间定位、在线检测并纠正注意力漂移的注意力监督推理机制，以及引导偏好以生成视觉上一致响应的视觉注意力指导的直接偏好优化（DPO）。实验表明，各组件均有效降低幻觉率，整体框架在多个基准测试中表现最优，幻觉率下降40%-60%，同时保持了模型的多模态通用能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态大语言模型在生成过程中常出现与图像内容不符的幻觉现象，现有方法多为结果导向，未能针对内部注意力机制的退化这一根本原因进行干预。本文旨在从注意力动态角度揭示并解决幻觉产生的内在机制。

Method: 提出ADAPT框架，包括：1）从早期解码阶段提取视觉锚点以稳定跨模态对齐；2）设计注意力监督推理机制，实时检测和修正注意力漂移；3）引入视觉注意力引导的直接偏好优化（DPO），使模型偏好更贴近视觉真实。

Result: ADAPT各组件均有效减少幻觉，完整框架在主流多模态模型上实现40%-60%的幻觉率降低，在多个基准测试中达到新最佳性能，且未损害模型的通用多模态理解能力。

Conclusion: 本研究从内部注意力动态视角出发，揭示了多模态模型幻觉的成因，并提出有效的干预策略。ADAPT框架为缓解幻觉提供了可解释、可扩展的方法路径，推动多模态生成的可靠性提升。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) are critically hampered by hallucination, generating content inconsistent with the provided image. In this paper, we identify an internal signature of hallucination: progressive degradation of text-to-image cross-attention during generation, leading to specific failure patterns like unfocused or biased attention. Existing mitigation strategies are largely outcome-driven and do not explicitly target this failure mode. To address this problem, we propose ADAPT (Attention Dynamics Alignment with Preference Tuning), an attention-based framework that intervenes directly on text-to-image cross-attention dynamics. We propose ADAPT with three key contributions: a cross-attention visual anchor refined from early decoding to provide stable spatial grounding, an attention-supervised inference mechanism that detects and corrects attention drift online, and a Visual Attention Guidance DPO that aligns preferences toward visually grounded responses. Experiments show that each component of ADAPT contributes to hallucination reduction, and the full framework achieves new best results across multiple hallucination benchmarks, reducing hallucination rates by 40%-60% across mainstream backbones while preserving general multimodal capabilities. Our work provides an attention-based perspective on mitigating hallucinations by exploring the model's internal text-to-image cross-attention behaviors. Code is available at https://github.com/yao-ustc/ADAPT

</details>


### [21] [Diffusion-Based Material Regularization for Physics-Based Inverse Rendering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31065)
*Jingwang Ling,Lifan Wu,Feng Xu,Shuang Zhao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种融合数据驱动扩散模型与物理基础逆渲染的新方法，通过将扩散模型的预测作为优化过程中的相似性核来正则化材质重建，从而在保持图像逼真度的同时满足渲染方程。该方法联合优化几何、材质和光照，实现高质量3D资产重建，可直接用于标准渲染与真实重照明，在多个基准数据集上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统物理逆渲染因缺乏强先验而面临严重欠约束问题，导致光照与材质耦合且泛化能力差；而数据驱动扩散模型虽能生成视觉逼真的材质，但不满足渲染方程，无法直接用于物理渲染。因此需要一种结合两者优势的方法，以实现既真实又可物理兼容的3D资产重建。

Method: 提出一种基于扩散模型预测作为相似性核的正则化损失：在扩散模型输出近似恒定的表面区域，限制优化过程中材质的剧烈变化，同时允许自由匹配输入图像。构建端到端框架，联合优化几何、材质和光照，确保结果符合渲染方程并可直接用于标准渲染管线。

Result: 在Synthetic4Relight、Stanford-ORB和DTC-Synthetic等数据集上，本方法在重建精度和重照明质量方面均显著超越现有最优基线方法，生成的3D资产具备良好的可编辑性和真实性。

Conclusion: 通过将扩散模型的预测用作优化过程中的正则化信号，而非直接作为目标值，本方法成功融合了数据驱动与物理模型的优势，实现了高保真、可物理渲染的3D资产重建，为真实感图形处理提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Reconstructing physics-based 3D assets -- geometry, materials, and illumination -- from multi-view images is a core problem in computer graphics and vision, and a prerequisite for realistic relighting and editing. Physics-based inverse rendering offers an accurate image-formation model, but is severely underconstrained: without strong priors, illumination is baked into materials, and reconstructions generalize poorly to novel views and lighting. Data-driven diffusion models, in contrast, predict visually plausible materials, yet their predictions rarely satisfy the rendering equation and are not directly usable for physics-based rendering. We bridge these two paradigms rather than replacing either. Our key idea is to treat the predictions of a state-of-the-art diffusion model not as target material values but as a similarity kernel for optimization: we introduce a regularization loss that penalizes deviations in the optimized material over surface regions where the diffusion predictions are near-constant, while leaving the optimization free to match the input images. Built on this regularizer, our end-to-end pipeline jointly reconstructs geometry, materials, and illumination, yielding high-quality assets that drop into standard rendering pipelines and relight faithfully. On the Synthetic4Relight, Stanford-ORB, and DTC-Synthetic datasets, our method significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in both reconstruction accuracy and relighting quality.

</details>


### [22] [Hybrid Unet-Transformer Model for Generating Stress and Strain Fields from Composite Geometrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31068)
*Shrey Patel*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种混合UNet-Transformer架构，可直接从复合材料微结构几何图像预测复杂的应力应变场分布，作为有限元方法（FEM）的高效替代模型。该模型在十种不同类型的应力/应变场预测中表现优异，尤其在周期性排列几何结构上达到R²=0.9991、SSIM=0.9936、MAE=0.0050的高精度。多数子数据集的MAE低于0.05（归一化[0,1]尺度），且通过Grad-CAM分析显示模型能自动聚焦于相界、连接节点等力学关键区域，具备物理合理性。但在不规则稀疏软相包含的方形网格结构上性能下降，表明其对尖锐应力突变的建模能力受限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统有限元方法（FEM）虽准确但计算成本极高，难以满足大规模材料设计需求；亟需发展高效、精准的替代模型以实现微结构到力学场的快速映射。

Conclusion: 所提出的混合架构为复杂复合材料微结构的力学场预测提供了一种高效、高精度的替代方案，具备良好的泛化能力与物理可解释性，适用于多类型复合材料的快速设计与优化，但对极端不规则结构仍需改进。

Abstract: Accurate prediction of stress and strain fields in hierarchical composite microstructures is critical for physics-informed material design, yet conventional finite element method (FEM) simulations are computationally prohibitive at scale, requiring minutes to days per evaluation. Results demonstrate that the proposed architecture achieves strong predictive performance across the majority of subdatasets, with peak accuracy on periodic tessellation geometries reaching R2=0.9991, SSIM=0.9936, and MAE=0.0050 on the boundary condition subdataset and the triangular tessellation subdataset respectively. Across six of the eight evaluated subdatasets, MAE remains below 0.05 on the normalized [0,1] pixel scale. Performance degrades on irregular square-grid geometries with sparse soft-phase inclusions, with the S11 normal stress subdataset yielding R2=0.7735 and SSIM=0.7126, consistent with the known limitation of smooth-loss image translation models in reproducing sharp stress discontinuities.

Abstract: Semantic navigation is a fundamental task for embodied agents operating in unseen environments, requiring both semantic understanding and long-term decision-making. Recent foundation models have empowered agents with rich semantic priors for this task. However, without structured global representations, decision-making often falls back on local observations and greedy strategies, resulting in inefficient exploration and myopic behaviors, especially in long-distance navigation. To address these challenges, we propose a zero-shot semantic navigation framework. Our method incrementally maintains an online Hierarchical 3D Scene Graph (HSG) to form a multi-granular semantic topology over objects, zones, and regions, serving as a compact state abstraction for global planning. Building on this memory, we introduce a hierarchical belief-based planning framework that fuses semantic priors with exploration evidence on the HSG, and performs finite-horizon rollouts on an HSG-based simulator to explicitly estimate the long-term expected returns of candidate macro-actions. This enables globally consistent decisions and reduces redundant backtracking. Extensive experiments in high-fidelity simulation environments across multiple tasks and datasets demonstrate that our method outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods, particularly in long-distance scenarios, where our approach improves SR and SPL by an average of 9.4\% and 5.0\%, respectively.

Crucially, our method provides annotations that strictly adhere to 3D geometric consistency through explicit 3D reprojection, avoiding SfM-MVS error accumulation. ### [25] [Fleet: Few Shots Lead Effective AI-generated Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31082)
*Jiaan Wang,Sirui Liu,Yu Li,Kaiyuan Yang,Juan Cao,Sheng Tang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Fleet框架，通过动态适应实现AI生成图像检测的持续少量样本演化，解决静态特征空间在新兴生成器面前表现崩溃的问题。引入受限路由修正机制，利用解耦子空间中的避让路由将新型AI样本引导至非真实图像主导路径，显著提升对现代生成器（如Doubao Seedream 4.0）的检测性能，从20.4%提升至73.1%，仅需10次样本适应。构建Treasure基准，涵盖64个模型与36万张图像，验证方法有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AIGI检测方法依赖静态特征空间假设，难以应对快速演化的生成器（如SD3、Nano Banana Pro），导致在新生成器上性能严重下降，亟需突破静态泛化范式，转向动态适应以实现持续防御能力。

Method: 提出Fleet框架，采用连续少数样本演化策略，用受限路由修正替代无约束特征更新；通过解耦子空间中的避免路由机制，将新型AI样本引导至非真实图像主导路径，实现对新兴威胁的快速对齐。

Result: 在Treasure基准上，静态先进方法在现代生成器上性能崩溃，而Fleet仅用10次样本适应，将检测准确率从20.4%大幅提升至73.1%，显著优于现有方法。

Conclusion: AIGI检测应从静态泛化转向动态适应，Fleet框架通过持续少量样本演化与受限路由修正，有效应对不断演化的生成威胁，为开放世界对抗防御提供了新范式。

Abstract: AI-generated image (AIGI) detection is undergoing a critical transition from laboratory benchmarks to open-world adversarial defense. The prevalent paradigm focuses on finding static feature spaces, assuming that some invariant artifacts learned from historical data can achieve universal zero-shot generalization. While achieving saturation on several AIGI benchmarks, this static hypothesis suffers a severe performance drop against rapidly evolving generators (e.g., SD3, Nano Banana Pro). To address these limitations, we propose that the field should expand beyond "static generalization" to a new paradigm of "dynamic adaptation". We introduce Fleet, a framework that pioneers a dynamic paradigm of continuous few-shot evolution, enabling rapid alignment with emerging generative threats. Fleet improves few-shot adaptation by replacing unconstrained feature updates with constrained routing correction, where avoidance routing redirects novel AI samples away from Non-AI-dominated routes within decoupled subspaces. To validate this, we present Treasure, a benchmark spanning 64 models and 360k images, featuring diverse architectures and 20 closed-source commercial engines. Experiments reveal that while static SOTA methods fail catastrophically on modern generators, Fleet restores performance from 20.4% to 73.1% with only 10-shot adaptation on "Doubao Seedream 4.0". Code and data are available at https://github.com/ICTMCG/Fleet .

### [29] [Do Not Break the Vessels: Structure-Preserving Mean Flow for Vascular Image Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31095)
*Changjin Sun,Zhuo Hu,Kaini Wang,Baixuan Wu,Shuo Gao,Runan Zheng,Cheng Xue,Yudong Zhang,Guangquan Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结构保持的均值流（SPMF）框架，将血管图像翻译建模为拓扑不变的传输过程，通过正交性约束分离外观传输与拓扑失真，结合布朗桥扩散模型在每一步保持拓扑结构；同时引入原型引导的结构精炼模块（PGSR），提升推理时结构与训练时结构的一致性。实验在NIRII到2PF和眼底数据集上均优于现有方法，分别达到24.96 dB和24.83 dB的峰值PSNR。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有跨模态图像翻译方法侧重像素级保真或视觉真实感，将结构保持视为输出结果的属性而非生成过程的不变性，导致结构不连续和伪影，影响解剖学一致性和临床可靠性。

Method: 提出结构保持的均值流（SPMF）框架，基于结构不变性原则推导出流速度场的正交性约束，实现外观传输与拓扑失真的分离；在布朗桥扩散模型中以时间加权代理目标实现每步扩散过程的拓扑保持；设计原型引导的结构精炼模块（PGSR），对齐推理时与训练时的结构。

Result: 在配对的NIRII-to-2PF和眼底数据集上，相比现有最先进方法取得一致改进，分别获得24.96 dB和24.83 dB的峰值PSNR，验证了方法的有效性与优越性。

Conclusion: 所提出的SPMF框架通过拓扑不变的生成过程有效保留血管结构，结合PGSR模块进一步提升结构一致性，显著改善跨模态血管图像重建的质量与临床可用性。

Abstract: Reconstructing anatomically faithful vascular structures from clinically accessible imaging modalities is of substantial clinical significance. However, existing cross-modal translation methods mainly emphasize pixel-level fidelity or visual realism and treat structure preservation as a property of the final output rather than an invariant of the generative process. This limitation often leads to structural discontinuities and artifacts, compromising anatomical coherence and clinical reliability. In this work, we propose a Structure-Preserving Mean Flow (SPMF) framework that formulates vascular image translation as a topology-invariant transport process. Based on a structural invariance principle, we derive an orthogonality constraint on the flow velocity field that formally separates appearance transport from topological distortion. We implement this constraint as a time-weighted surrogate objective within a Brownian bridge diffusion model to preserve topology at every diffusion step. Moreover, we propose a Prototype-Guided Structural Refinement (PGSR) module to align degraded inference-time structures with reliable training-time structures. Experiments on paired NIRII-to-2PF and fundus datasets demonstrate consistent improvements over state-of-the-art methods, achieving peak PSNR values of 24.96 dB and 24.83 dB, respectively.

*Geonho Bang,Geunju Baek,Dongyoung Lee,Wonjun Jeong,Jun Won Choi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Horizon3D提出了一种基于高斯原型的稀疏雷达-相机融合框架，用于长距离3D目标检测。通过关键点引导的高斯初始化、面向对象的稀疏融合以及双路径时序融合，有效结合了物体级细节与场景级上下文，在保持高效推理速度的同时显著提升了检测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有雷达-相机融合方法在长距离检测中面临计算开销大、细节丢失和时序信息利用不足的问题，尤其在高速自动驾驶场景下难以兼顾精度与效率。

Method: Horizon3D采用高斯原型初始化于雷达与相机估计的目标关键点，通过对象中心稀疏融合优化高斯表示，并将其投射到BEV平面以融合稀疏雷达BEV上下文；同时引入双路径时序融合机制，分别在BEV路径中积累场景级时序信息，在高斯路径中传播对象级运动信息。

Result: 在TruckScenes数据集上，Horizon3D达到当前最优性能，在验证集上相比前人最佳方法提升+3.0 NDS和+1.6 mAP，且推理速度具有竞争力。

Conclusion: Horizon3D成功实现了长距离雷达-相机融合3D目标检测中精度与效率的平衡，为自动驾驶中的远距离感知提供了有效解决方案。

Abstract: Long-range 3D object detection is critical for safe autonomous driving at highway speeds, yet existing radar-camera fusion methods remain limited at extended ranges. BEV-based methods capture scene-level context but incur rapidly growing computation and often lose fine-grained object detail, while query-based methods are efficient but provide limited scene-level context. Temporal fusion further requires both multi-frame accumulation for sparse distant observations and object-level motion modeling for fast-moving objects. We propose Horizon3D, a sparse radar-camera fusion framework for long-range 3D object detection that combines Gaussian primitives with sparse BEV features. Horizon3D initializes Gaussian primitives at radar- and camera-estimated object keypoints using Keypoint-Guided Gaussian Initialization, refines them through Object-Centric Sparse Fusion, and splats them onto the BEV plane to fuse object-level detail with sparse radar BEV context. It further introduces Dual-Path Temporal Fusion, which aggregates temporal cues through a BEV path for scene-level accumulation and a Gaussian path for object-level motion propagation. Experiments on TruckScenes show that Horizon3D achieves state-of-the-art radar-camera 3D detection performance. On the validation set, it outperforms the previous best method by +3.0 NDS and +1.6 mAP while maintaining competitive inference speed.

</details>


### [31] [PiLoT v2: Pixel-to-Orthogonal Map Alignment for Free-view UAV Geo-localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31098)
*Xinyi Liu,Xiaoya Cheng,Rouwan Wu,Zhaochen Wang,Shen Yan,Maojun Zhang,Yu Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: PiLoT v2 提出了一种轻量级、鲁棒的无人机地理定位系统，通过直接像素到正射地图注册实现无漂移实时定位。它利用真数字正射影像图（TDOM）和数字地表模型（DSM）替代高成本3D渲染，显著降低存储与计算开销，并通过跨视角特征注册网络解决视图差异问题，同时结合机载传感器先验提升鲁棒性，在性能接近甚至超越PiLoT的同时大幅优化部署可行性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统PiLoT依赖复杂的3D网格，导致存储大、建图复杂、渲染成本高，难以在嵌入式平台部署，亟需更高效、轻量化的解决方案以支持无人机在无GNSS环境下的自主飞行。

Method: 采用真数字正射影像图（TDOM）与数字地表模型（DSM）作为参考基底，将3D渲染替换为高效的CPU友好的地图裁剪操作；构建大规模几何标注数据集训练跨视角特征注册网络以补偿2.5D正射图与自由视角航拍图像之间的几何差异；将重力方向和单点激光测距等机载传感器先验融入姿态优化流形中，增强对视觉退化情况的鲁棒性。

Result: 实验表明，PiLoT v2 在定位精度上达到或超过原版PiLoT，同时在存储占用和计算成本方面有显著降低，具备更强的嵌入式部署能力。

Conclusion: PiLoT v2 成功实现了从依赖3D渲染到基于2.5D正射地图的范式转变，兼顾高精度与低资源消耗，是面向嵌入式无人机自主导航的理想选择。

Abstract: Real-time, drift-free UAV geo-localization is essential for autonomous missions in GNSS-denied environments. The pioneering system, PiLoT, achieves high precision via Neural Pixel-to-3D Registration, aligning UAV video streams with a single rendered reference view from 3D meshes. However, its reliance on heavy 3D meshes incurs massive storage overheads, complex map acquisition, and significant computational rendering costs, severely hindering deployment on embedded platforms. To address these bottlenecks, we propose PiLoT v2, a lightweight yet robust evolution that shifts the paradigm to direct pixel-to-orthogonal map registration for free-view UAV geo-localization. By leveraging True Digital Orthophoto Maps (TDOMs) and Digital Surface Models (DSMs) as the reference substrate, PiLoT v2 replaces GPU-intensive 3D rendering with a highly efficient, CPU-friendly map cropping operation. To bridge the severe geometric discrepancy between these 2.5D orthogonal crops and free-view oblique UAV imagery, we train a cross-view feature registration network using a novel, large-scale geometrically annotated dataset. Furthermore, we integrate onboard sensor prior--specifically gravity direction and single-point laser rang--directly into the pose optimization manifold to enhance robustness against cross-view visual degradation. Experimental results demonstrate that PiLoT v2 achieves performance comparable to, or even exceeding, its Pixel-to-3D predecessor, while offering drastically lower storage and computational costs.

To this end, we introduce View-PNDF (View-specific Pattern Neuron Detection and Fine-tuning), a parameter-efficient framework that fosters view-consistent report generation from a neuronal perspective. Specifically, View-PNDF comprises: (i) a view-specific neuron detection module identifying neurons responsive to particular views, (ii) a verification module quantifying the existence of these neurons, and (iii) a selective fine-tuning strategy strengthening detected neurons while preserving view-agnostic representations. By updating only view-specific neurons, View-PNDF achieves consistent diagnoses across different views with reduced computational costs. Subsequently, we employ Large Language Models (LLMs) to consolidate the view-specific reports into a complete radiology report. Furthermore, we use traditional Natural Language Generation (NLG) metrics-based assessment on integrated reports for baseline comparison and employ LLM-based assessment (e.g., GPT-4o) on view-specific reports to capture clinical significance. ### [33] [TaxoMIL: Taxonomy-Constrained Learning for Hierarchical Whole Slide Image Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31100)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统WSI诊断方法将滑片级诊断视为离散标签的平坦分类任务，忽略了临床推理中固有的层次性与粗粒度到细粒度的特性；现有层次分类器和视觉-语言模型存在语义不连贯或文本生成失控导致的分类幻觉与父子标签矛盾问题。

Method: 设计TaxoMIL框架，采用双头Transformer解码器分别生成粗粒度与细粒度诊断文本，并引入基于临床分类体系的约束目标，对标签嵌入空间进行结构化建模，严格约束视觉表示在分类树中的位置。

Abstract: Whole slide image (WSI) analysis is central to computational pathology, with multiple instance learning (MIL) emerging as the standard pipeline for slide-level diagnosis. However, conventional approaches formulate WSI diagnosis as a flat classification task over discrete labels, contradicting the inherently hierarchical, coarse-to-fine nature of clinical reasoning. Although recent hierarchical classifiers and vision-language models (VLMs) have sought to address this structural gap, they either fail to capture semantic continuity between related diagnoses or suffer from unconstrained text generation that produces taxonomic hallucinations and parent-child label violations. To address these limitations, we propose TaxoMIL, a taxonomy-constrained framework that reformulates WSI diagnosis as a multi-granularity text generation task. TaxoMIL utilizes a dual-head Transformer decoder to generate coarse- and fine-level diagnostic text, and introduces taxonomy-guided objectives that explicitly structure the label embedding space and strictly ground slide-level visual representations within the clinical taxonomy. Extensive experiments across three diverse WSI datasets demonstrate that TaxoMIL consistently outperforms state-of-the-art MIL classifiers and VLM-based generative methods, yielding accurate and hierarchy-aware diagnostic predictions. The code is released at https://github.com/QuIIL/TaxoMIL

### [34] [InfiniVerse: Occupancy Guided Unbounded Scene Generation for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31109)

Method: 首先从输入多视角帧重建3D占据表示；基于该表示进行沿任意轨迹的自回归场景扩展；利用视频扩散模型将粗略占据网格转化为逼真、时空一致的视频序列；提出分层草图-精炼范式，通过重投影生成视频作为图像条件反馈以增强3D占据表示，实现跨模态对齐与相互增强

Abstract: Generating realistic, controllable, and temporally coherent urban environments is a critical yet unresolved challenge in the autonomous driving community. In this paper, we introduce InfiniVerse, a unified pipeline for long-range, 2D-3D-aligned, and controllable synthesis of dynamic urban scenes from a single frame. In practice, our approach first reconstructs a 3D occupancy representation from the input multi-view frame. This representation serves as a foundation for autoregressive scene extension along arbitrary trajectories. Subsequently, a video diffusion model translates the coarse occupancy grid into realistic, spatiotemporally consistent video sequences. Moreover, we propose a hierarchical sketch-and-refine paradigm, in which the generated videos are re-projected as image-conditioned feedback to enhance the 3D occupancy representation, establishing cross-modal alignment and mutual enhancement between the visual and spatial domains. ### [35] [JacobianAvatar: Temporally Consistent Semi-rigid Avatar Reconstruction from a Monocular Video](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31115)
*Changyeon Won,Min-Gyu Park,Seonghwan Park,Ju Hong Yoon,Hae-Gon Jeon*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于神经雅可比场（NJFs）的方法，用于在单目条件下生成复杂动作中具有真实感的人类虚拟形象，尤其关注衣物动态等局部与全局变形。通过自监督神经网络预测随姿态变化的雅可比矩阵，并求解泊松方程来建模变形。针对单目输入带来的遮挡和不可见表面问题，引入三个关键组件：约束泊松求解器、基于符号距离的雅可比正则化以及变形引导的残差流损失，有效抑制边界伪影，恢复腋下、大腿等频繁遮挡区域，并保证运动过程中的时序一致性。实验在基准数据集和真实场景视频上验证了该方法在时序稳定性和几何一致性上的优越性，优于现有最先进方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在单目条件下生成具有真实感的人类虚拟形象，尤其是包含复杂运动如衣物动态的场景，面临全局与局部变形建模的挑战。同时，单目输入存在自遮挡和不可见表面等问题，导致重建质量下降。因此，需要一种能够有效处理这些困难的新方法。

Method: 采用神经雅可比场（NJFs）表示半刚性变形；训练自监督神经网络预测姿态相关的雅可比矩阵，并通过求解泊松方程实现变形建模；引入约束泊松求解器以处理边界问题，使用基于符号距离的雅可比正则化增强对隐藏区域的恢复能力，设计变形引导的残差流损失以保持时序一致性。

Result: 在多个基准数据集和真实场景视频上，所提方法生成的虚拟形象在时序稳定性与几何一致性方面表现优异，显著优于当前最先进的方法，尤其在恢复被遮挡区域（如腋下、大腿）方面效果突出。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种基于神经雅可比场的单目人类虚拟形象生成方法，通过创新的三个模块有效解决了单目输入下的遮挡与变形建模难题，实现了高质量、高稳定性的动态虚拟形象生成，为未来虚拟角色动画与交互应用提供了新思路。

Abstract: Generating realistic human avatars in complex motions--such as clothing dynamics--requires modeling of global and local deformations which remains challenging in monocular settings. We address this problem by leveraging neural Jacobian fields (NJFs) for representing semi-rigid deformations. We train self-supervised neural networks for predicting Jacobian matrices that give the pose-dependent deformations, by solving a Poisson equation. However, monocular input presents several difficulties such as self-occluded regions and invisible surfaces. To address these issues, we introduce three key components: a constrained Poisson solver, signed distance-based Jacobian regularization, and a deformation-guided residual flow loss, which together suppress boundary artifacts, recover frequently occluded regions such as armpits and thighs, and enforce temporal consistency during motion. Experiments on benchmark and in-the-wild videos demonstrate that our method generates temporally stable and geometrically coherent avatars, outperforming state-of-the-art approaches.

### [36] [WildProp: Visual Estimation of Wildlife Body Proportions at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31125)
*Mustafa Chasmai,Aaron Sun,Subhransu Maji*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: WildProp 是一种无需训练的框架，可直接从大规模、非受限图像库中估计野生动物体型比例分布。它通过姿态感知检索和密集补丁级匹配，将用户标注的参考图像中的部分端点转移至其他图像，并利用几何一致性过滤预测结果，最终聚合多个图像的测量值以获得种群级别的比例分布。该方法适用于任意物种和自定义部位，无需针对特定物种进行训练，在鸟类和两栖动物的多个数据集上取得了10-20%的中位相对误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统形态测量依赖受控成像或实体标本处理，难以规模化；现有监督关键点方法需为每种物种单独训练，限制了通用性与扩展性。因此亟需一种无需训练、可跨物种泛化、适用于大规模图像数据的形态测量新方法。

Method: 将形态测量建模为检索驱动的对应问题：基于用户标注的参考图像，利用基础模型特征进行姿态感知图像检索，通过密集补丁级匹配转移部件端点，采用几何一致性过滤预测结果，并对检索图像进行测量聚合以估计种群比例分布。

Result: 在三个涵盖鸟类和两栖动物的大规模形态数据集上，中位相对误差为10-20%。案例研究显示其可应用于鸟、蛙、昆虫、花等多种类群的多种比例测量。消融实验表明姿态感知检索对稳定估计至关重要，而鲁棒聚合能有效缓解关键点与姿态噪声的影响。

Conclusion: 经过精心筛选的2D对应关系，结合网络规模图像，可为跨分类群、地理区域和季节性的比较与子组分析提供可扩展的形态测量代理指标。

Abstract: Population-level morphometric measurements underpin ecological and evolutionary studies but traditionally require controlled imaging or physical specimen handling, limiting scalability. We present WildProp, a training-free framework that estimates wildlife body proportion distributions directly from large-scale, unconstrained image repositories. We cast morphometric estimation as a retrieval-driven correspondence problem: given a single user-annotated canonical image, WildProp performs pose-aware retrieval using foundation model features, transfers part endpoints via dense patch-level matching, filters predictions using geometric consistency, and aggregates measurements across retrieved images to estimate population-level ratio distributions. Unlike supervised keypoint pipelines, our approach adapts to arbitrary species and user-defined parts without per-species training. Evaluations on three large morphometric datasets spanning birds and amphibians show median relative errors of 10-20%. We further highlight the broad applicability of our approach through a number of case studies measuring various proportions across diverse taxa, including birds, frogs, insects, and flowers. Ablations demonstrate that pose-aware retrieval is critical for stable estimation, while robust aggregation mitigates keypoint and pose noise. Our results indicate that carefully curated 2D correspondences over web-scale imagery can provide scalable morphometric proxies for comparative and subgroup analyses across taxa, geography, and seasonality.

### [37] [SkillSpotter: Pose-Aware Multi-View Skilled Action Detection and Grading in Ego-Exo Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31127)
*Björn Braun,Christian Holz*

Conclusion: SkillSpotter为实时个性化教练系统提供了有效解决方案，显著提升了在复杂多视角环境下对技能动作的检测与质量评估能力，具有良好的可扩展性和泛化性。

In an ego-exo video setting, this requires simultaneously detecting individual skilled actions and classifying each as correct or needing improvement, which Ego-Exo4D's proficiency demonstration benchmark formalized. We first adapt seven state-of-the-art temporal action detection architectures to this task, extend the evaluation protocol to disentangle detection from grading, and show that existing methods grade near-randomly. We then introduce SkillSpotter, a pose-aware multi-view architecture that jointly detects and grades skilled actions through three task-specific modules: (1) adaptive temporal suppression to handle the varying density of skilled actions across diverse activities, (2) gated 3D body pose fusion to leverage body kinematics as a complementary signal to visual features, and (3) bidirectional cross-view attention to combine ego and exo views effectively. SkillSpotter improves class-specific mAP from 12.40 to 21.82 (+76%) and balanced accuracy from 55.99% to 60.40% over the best baseline. SkillSpotter's modules transfer to other temporal action detection models with consistent gains, and our method generalizes beyond Ego-Exo4D to HoloAssist. Code: https://github.com/eth-siplab/SkillSpotter

</details>


### [38] [MSNN-LINet: Cross-Modal Learning via Continuous Linear Integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31135)
*Gabriel Clinger*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LINet 是一种用于 RGB-D 场景分类的多流神经网络，通过线性集成卷积（LIConv2d）实现跨模态的连续融合，避免了传统融合方法的局限性。它采用三个并行流（RGB、深度、集成），在每个层级进行融合，并通过 1/N 初始化和渐进式模态丢弃来解决梯度传播问题和路径坍缩。在 SUN RGB-D 数据集上达到 45.2% 的平均分类准确率，使用 ScanNet 预训练可提升至 49.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多模态融合方法存在结构上的权衡：早期融合过早纠缠特征，晚期融合延迟融合时机，混合或注意力机制需要人为设计融合位置，缺乏系统性。本文旨在提出一种支持连续跨模态学习的架构，以更自然地整合多源信息。

Method: 提出 LINet 架构，包含三个并行流：RGB、深度和集成流。引入线性集成卷积（LIConv2d），在非线性激活前完成跨模态融合，实现每层的连续融合。采用 1/N 常数初始化缓解梯度混乱问题，并设计渐进式模态丢弃策略，防止路径坍缩。

Result: 在 SUN RGB-D 19 类场景分类任务中，从零训练达到 45.2% 的平均准确率，优于以往从头训练的方法；结合 ScanNet 预训练后提升至 49.6%。

Conclusion: LINet 通过连续融合与稳健的初始化及训练策略，有效提升了 RGB-D 场景分类性能，证明了持续跨模态学习在多模态视觉任务中的潜力。

Abstract: We present LINet (Linear Integration Network), a Multi-Stream Neural Network (MSNN) for RGB-D scene classification. Current multi-modal architectures treat feature fusion as a discrete, ad-hoc event: early fusion entangles representations prematurely, late fusion isolates them until the final layer, and hybrid or attention-based methods require architectural guesswork to place intermediate fusion blocks. LINet addresses this structural compromise by maintaining three dedicated parallel streams (RGB, depth, and integration) where a novel Linear Integration Convolution (LIConv2d) operator enables continuous cross-modal learning at every layer. The integration stream receives raw filtered signals from both modality streams and combines them before the nonlinear activation threshold, conceptually inspired by somatic integration preceding the neuronal firing decision. Implementing continuous integration exposes a critical initialization pathology: Kaiming initialization of the bridging weights scrambles gradients before they reach the stream backbones, producing a failure mode that resembles overfitting but is corrupted gradient flow. A 1/N constant initialization mitigates this. We employ progressive modality dropout, a curriculum adapted to continuous fusion in which blanking probability increases from zero, preventing pathway collapse, a form of negative co-learning, by forcing robust independent stream representations. Trained from scratch on SUN RGB-D 19-class scene classification, LINet reaches 45.2% mean class accuracy at ResNet18 scale, outperforming prior from-scratch results, and rises to 49.6% with in-domain RGB-D (ScanNet) pretraining.

### [39] [FROST: Training-Free Few-Shot Segmentation with Frozen Features and Nonparametric Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31136)
*Junghwan Park*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FROST 是一种无需训练的少样本分割方法，专为遥感影像设计。它利用冻结的 DINOv3 特征，将参考图像中的前景和背景视为单位球面上的点云，通过非参数密度比进行查询图像中每个标记的分类，并基于贝叶斯规则设定零阈值。该方法能有效保留多模态类别的内部结构，随着参考样本增多，决策逐渐清晰，所有参数均来自支持集而非人工调参。在17个遥感基准测试中，FROST 在单样本情况下领先5.6 mIoU，且模型体积小，性能持续提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遥感领域标签稀缺，且影像与自然图像差异大，现有方法或受限于训练分布，或使用损失严重的特征摘要（如单一原型），无法保留多模态类别的内部结构。因此需要一种能直接建模类别分布、无需训练、并保持高精度的方法。

Method: FROST 将参考图像的前景和背景表示为冻结 DINOv3 特征空间中的点云，采用非参数密度比估计进行像素级分类；通过贝叶斯规则设定零阈值，使决策随支持集增大而增强；所有超参数（如核带宽、空间门控）均由支持集自适应确定，无需人工调优。

Result: 在17个遥感基准上，FROST 在仅一个标注样本时即实现5.6 mIoU 的领先优势，并随支持集增长进一步扩大领先；同时模型尺寸最小，优于现有训练自由与学习型方法。

Conclusion: FROST 证明了以分布而非点来描述类别在少样本分割中的优越性，尤其适用于遥感中由多个小而异质实例组成的复杂类别。其无需训练、自适应性强、高效且精准，是少样本分割在遥感场景下的新标杆。

Abstract: Few-shot segmentation asks a model to delineate a target class in a query image from only a handful of annotated examples, a setting most acute in remote sensing, where labels are scarce and the imagery departs sharply from the natural images on which vision backbones are pretrained. Prevailing approaches either train a segmenter on labelled episodes, which raises accuracy within the training distribution but binds the model to it, or reduce each class to a lossy summary of frozen features, a single prototype, a few cluster prototypes, or a discrete clustering, none of which preserves the internal structure of a multimodal class. We argue that a class is better described by a distribution than by a point, and that frozen self-supervised features already carry enough structure to estimate that distribution directly. We introduce FROST, a training-free few-shot segmenter that treats the reference foreground and background as two point clouds on the unit sphere of frozen DINOv3 features and labels each query token by a nonparametric density ratio, with a threshold the Bayes rule fixes at zero under equal priors. Because the variance of a density estimate shrinks as its sample grows, the decision sharpens as references accumulate, and every remaining quantity from the kernel bandwidth to the spatial gate is read from the support set rather than tuned. We develop FROST for overhead imagery, where a class is typically a scatter of many small and dissimilar instances that a density tracks but a lossy summary blurs. Across seventeen remote-sensing benchmarks FROST surpasses both training-free and learning-based methods, leading by 5.6 mIoU from a single annotated example and widening its lead as the support set grows, all while remaining among the smallest models compared. Code is available at https://github.com/jhpark-ai/FROST.

### [40] [WaterGen: Decoupling Scene and Medium in Underwater Image Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31147)
*Jiayi Wu,Tianfu Wang,Tianyi Xiong,Dehao Yuan,Xiaomin Lin,Md Jahidul Islam,Cornelia Fermuller,Christopher Metzler,Yiannis Aloimonos*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Underwater computer vision tasks, such as detection, restoration, and segmentation, are limited by the scarcity of large-scale and diverse training data. We introduce WaterGen, a method for generating large-scale, realistic, and diverse underwater images that provides independent control of the scene and water medium conditions. Our approach treats underwater image generation as the decoupled control of two factors: realistic and diverse scene content (what is in the image), and accurate and controllable water medium effects (what the water does to the image). Existing methods generally achieve only part of this objective: they either provide controllability with limited realism or diversity, or generate realistic scenes without accurately and independently modeling water-medium effects. Our key insight, that allows us to avoid this compromise, is that scene generation and medium modeling can be decoupled within a latent diffusion framework, enabling diverse scene generation together with accurate and controllable underwater appearance. To do this, we decompose underwater image synthesis into two stages. First, we fine-tune the latent diffusion U-Net using degradation-free underwater images so that it learns to generate diverse and realistic latent embeddings of underwater scene content without medium-induced degradation. Second, we formulate the physically accurate medium degradation synthesis as a conditional decoding process applied to these latent embeddings. This decoupled design allows our model to generate diverse scenes with full control of underwater appearance. We leverage WaterGen to build large-scale synthetic underwater datasets that are diverse in scene structures and accurate in water effects and pseudo-labels. We demonstrate that our synthetic data consistently improve downstream performance in underwater restoration and semantic segmentation.

Abstract: 3D Visual Grounding (3DVG) aims to localize target objects in 3D scenes given natural language descriptions. Existing approaches typically perform reasoning over the entire scene, leading to ambiguous predictions and high computational cost, especially in cluttered environments. We observe that many referential expressions rely on local spatial context and often correspond to restricted spatial regions rather than the full scene. Motivated by this insight, we propose PruneGround, an effective plug-and-play framework for 3DVG built upon three key components. First, we introduce Language-Guided Spatial Pruning (LGSP), which leverages a frozen Vision Language Model (VLM) to identify language-relevant regions, thereby reducing spatial computation and grounding candidates in the narrower search space. Second, we propose MultiView-Conditioned Description Reformulation (MCDR), which decomposes complex expressions into simplified target-anchor relations and augments missing spatial cues through multi-view reasoning. Finally, we propose LLM-Grounder, which repurposes a detection-pretrained spatial LLM into a language-conditioned grounding model by aligning point cloud and linguistic representations within the pruned region. Extensive experiments on the three most popular point cloud benchmarks demonstrate that our method achieves state-of-the-art results on all three ScanRefer settings and on 9 out of 10 Nr3D/Sr3D settings.
