Abstract: Accurate energy demand forecasting is essential for the reliable operation and planning of modern sustainable energy systems. Spatial-temporal graph neural networks (STGNNs) have recently achieved strong performance in point forecasting by jointly modeling temporal dynamics and relational dependencies across interconnected energy nodes. However, in real-world energy systems, accurate point forecasts alone are insufficient, as operators also require reliable uncertainty estimates to support risk-aware decision-making, grid stability, and operational planning under uncertainty. Conformal prediction provides a principled and model-agnostic framework for uncertainty quantification with statistical coverage guarantees, making it particularly attractive for safety-critical energy applications. However, existing conformal prediction approaches often fail to fully capture the complex spatial-temporal structure of energy systems. To address these limitations, we propose STOIC (Spatial-Temporal Graph Conformal Prediction with In-Context Learning), a novel framework that integrates graph-based forecasting with the zero-shot calibration capabilities of tabular foundation models. STOIC first generates point forecasts using an STGNN and subsequently reformulates spatial-temporal residuals into a tabular representation suitable for in-context learning. Leveraging a tabular foundation model, STOIC calibrates prediction intervals without task-specific retraining, effectively capturing both sequential and relational dependencies. We evaluate STOIC on five diverse benchmarks, including synthetic simulations as well as real-world electricity and district heating networks. Across all datasets, STOIC consistently outperforms existing conformal prediction baselines, delivering more reliable and robust uncertainty estimates for complex graph-structured energy time series.

### [349] [Review Residuals: Update-Conditioned Residual Gating for Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31859)
*Kyle Kramer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出Review Residuals，通过学习输入相关的门控机制来动态调整残差更新，显著提升深层网络训练稳定性，并在大模型规模下表现出超越标准残差和Highway门控的性能优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有残差连接采用固定系数1进行叠加，无法评估更新的可靠性；受人因工程中独立验证原则启发，旨在引入可学习、依赖输入的门控机制以提升模型鲁棒性与训练效果。

Method: 设计一种新型残差结构：h_l = h_{l-1} + r_l * u_l，其中门控信号r_l由基于RMSNorm归一化后的当前状态和提议更新联合计算的sigmoid函数生成，实现输入依赖的自适应缩放。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在深度网络中具有更好的稳定性（可稳定训练至超深层数），且在大规模模型（590M及以上）上显著优于标准残差和参数匹配的Highway门控结构，性能随模型规模增长而增强。

Conclusion: Review Residuals通过引入输入依赖的门控机制，有效解决了深层网络训练中的梯度消失问题，并在大模型尺度下展现出显著且持续的优势，证明了其在规模化建模中的有效性。

Abstract: Residual connections add every sublayer's proposed update with a fixed coefficient of one; the network never evaluates whether an update is reliable before committing it. Drawing on the human-factors principle of independent verification, we introduce Review Residuals, which scale each update by a learned, input-dependent gate conditioned on both the current state and the proposed update: h_l = h_{l-1} + r_l * u_l with r_l = sigmoid(W[RMSNorm(h_{l-1}), RMSNorm(u_l)]). Conditioning the gate on the update is the property that distinguishes it from prior gated and scaled residuals. We report two findings. First, a depth-stability result: a convex (Highway-style) form of the gate reintroduces vanishing gradients and fails to train beyond ~20 layers, whereas the additive, identity-preserving form trains stably at all depths we tested. Second, an emergence-with-scale result: trained from scratch across five sizes (60M-1B parameters, multi-seed), Review Residuals show no advantage at small scale but at 590M significantly outperform both a parameter-matched Highway gate and a parameter-matched standard residual (p<0.05), with a larger advantage at 1B. The benefit grows with model size rather than shrinking.

</details>


### [350] [Geometry-Preserving Orthonormal Initialization for Low-Rank Adaptation in RLVR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31813)
*Ruijia Zhang,Jiacheng Zhu,Hanqing Zhu,Laixi Shi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了低秩适配（LoRA）及其变体在强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）框架下的表现，发现现有结构化初始化方法（如PiSSA和MiLoRA）在RLVR中可能表现不佳甚至导致训练不稳定。通过理论分析，作者证明正交初始化能最小化LoRA与全量微调之间的差距，并提出几何保持的正交初始化方法，设计出两种新变体RLPO和RLMO。实验表明，新方法在数学推理任务上显著提升稳定性与性能，优于标准LoRA，且解释了原有方法失效的原因。代码与模型已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有低秩适配方法（如PiSSA和MiLoRA）在监督微调下表现优异，但在强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）场景中效果不佳，甚至出现训练不稳，说明当前的低秩矩阵初始化策略在RLVR中缺乏理论支持，亟需更合理的初始化机制以保障训练稳定性和性能。

Method: 提出几何保持的正交初始化策略，基于理论分析证明正交初始化可最小化LoRA与全量微调之间的差距；据此设计两种新变体RLPO和RLMO，并在数学推理基准上进行实验验证其有效性。

Result: 所提方法在多个数学推理基准上显著提升了RLVR训练的稳定性，性能超越标准LoRA及原有变体（PiSSA、MiLoRA），并成功解释了后者在RLVR中表现不佳的内在原因。

Conclusion: 正交初始化在RLVR中具有理论优势，几何保持的正交初始化可有效提升低秩适配在强化学习场景中的表现，为高效、稳定的参数高效微调提供了新范式。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation (LoRA) and its variants enable parameter-efficient fine-tuning of large language models under the supervised fine-tuning (SFT) paradigm. However, their efficacy and behavior under Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) are less well understood. In particular, two structurally initialized LoRA variants, PiSSA and MiLoRA, which outperform standard LoRA under SFT, can underperform standard LoRA under RLVR and may even exhibit training instability. These observations suggest that how to initialize the low-rank matrices in RLVR remains unclear. In this work, we develop a theoretical analysis of LoRA in RLVR, showing that orthonormal initialization achieves the minimal gap between LoRA outcome and that of full fine-tuning. Guided by this insight, we propose geometry-preserving orthonormal initialization for low-rank adaptation in RLVR, leading to two new variants, RLPO and RLMO. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that the proposed orthonormal initialization stabilizes RLVR training and outperforms standard LoRA, contrasting with PiSSA and MiLoRA. Finally, our unified analysis for LoRA initialization also explains why PiSSA and MiLoRA can underperform in RLVR, which may be of independent interest. Code and checkpoints are publicly available at https://github.com/Richard-ZZZ/geometry-preserving-orthonormal-init-rlvr.

### [351] [Signed-Permutation Coordinate Transport for RMSNorm Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31963)
*John Sweeney*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了现代大模型工作流中坐标索引对象在检查点间的传输问题，指出残差流的规范选择（gauge）对齐至关重要。不同架构（LayerNorm vs RMSNorm）对应不同的对称性：LayerNorm为置换对称群 $S_d$，RMSNorm为带符号的置换群 $B_d$。传统仅考虑置换的对齐方法在RMSNorm模型中不完整。提出‘符号边缘化匈牙利匹配’以克服原始相关性匹配的精度上限，并证明其有效性。通过沿相同基础微调轨迹组合局部 $B_d$ 规范，实现了91.1%的坐标恢复率（远超60.3%的端点匹配），且该提升不能仅由基线路由解释。进一步验证了该方法在稀疏自编码器重建、情感引导向量、拒绝引导向量等任务中的优越表现，以及对AdamW状态重启动轨迹的正确保持。最后强调：所有索引级可解释性结论必须相对于明确的规范定义才有意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型工作流中跨检查点的坐标索引对象（如引导向量、神经元集合等）传输依赖于模型残差流的规范选择。然而，当前方法未充分考虑不同归一化架构（特别是RMSNorm）带来的符号-置换对称性，导致对齐不完整，进而影响可解释性与模型合并的可靠性。因此亟需建立正确的规范框架以实现真正的坐标保持传输。

Method: 提出符号边缘化匈牙利匹配算法；构建基于局部 $B_d$ 规范的坐标追踪机制；沿同源微调路径组合规范以恢复跨运行坐标；通过大量实验对比端点匹配与坐标保持策略；引入规范扫描审计以检验可重复性。

Result: 坐标保持传输在1500步时恢复率达91.1%，显著优于端点匹配的60.3%；在稀疏自编码器重建、情感/拒绝引导向量中性能大幅提升（如重建误差从1.08降至0.004，引导效果保留率从17.2%升至95.8%）；签名保持的AdamW状态能准确恢复训练轨迹；规范不一致导致可解释性结论不可复现。

Conclusion: 坐标保持传输必须基于正确的 $B_d$ 规范而非仅 $S_d$ 置换对齐。只有显式定义并遵循规范，才能实现跨检查点的可靠坐标传递与可解释性分析。该框架提升了模型合并、工具迁移与训练恢复的准确性与一致性。

Abstract: Modern LLM workflows move coordinate-indexed objects across checkpoints: steering vectors, sparse autoencoders, top-$k$ neuron sets, attribution lists, and merge alignments. This is only well posed after fixing the model's residual-stream gauge, which we show is architecture-dependent: LayerNorm residual charts have permutation gauge $S_d$ (up to a global sign flip), while RMSNorm charts with generic per-channel gain have signed-permutation gauge $B_d = S_d \ltimes \{\pm 1\}^d$. Permutation-only alignment is therefore symmetry-incomplete for RMSNorm models. We introduce sign-marginalized Hungarian matching and prove a sharp failure mode: with decorrelated coordinates, raw signed-correlation matching has a structural permutation-accuracy ceiling at the positive-sign fraction of the true gauge, which sign-marginalization removes. We then make coordinate-preserving transport, not function-level merging, the primary object: composing saved-checkpoint local $B_d$ gauges along same-base fine-tuning trajectories recovers 91.1% of cross-run coordinates at 1500 steps versus 60.3% for endpoint matching, and the gain is not explained by merely routing through the base. The recovered gauge transfers tools that permutation-only alignment breaks: TinyLlama SAE reconstruction has NMSE 0.004 under $B_d$ versus 1.08 under $S_d$; Qwen sentiment steering preserves 95.8% of its effect versus 17.2%; refusal steering reverses sign under $S_d$; coordinate-preserving merges behave the same way. The same covariance governs stateful training: signed transport of AdamW state preserves the resumed trajectory, while permutation-only state follows a different one from a functionally identical checkpoint. Finally, gauge-sweep audits show index-level interpretability claims are reproducible only relative to an explicit gauge.

</details>


### [352] [Low-dimensional topology of deep neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31856)
*Junyu Ren,Lek-Heng Lim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了在宽度限制为3的层模型（如前馈网络、ResNets和transformers）中，如何通过低维拓扑不变量（特别是链接数）来分析神经网络各层对拓扑结构的影响。通过将表示空间限制在ℝ³，避免了高维空间中拓扑结构被平凡化的问题，从而能更清晰地观察深度与激活函数的作用。研究发现：ResNet中的跳跃连接与transformer中的注意力机制在改变链接数方面具有同等能力；ResNets和transformers比使用单调激活函数的前馈网络更强；而后者又优于可逆模型和流模型；若将单调激活替换为非单调激活，则前馈网络可达到与ResNets和transformers相同的表达能力。该研究揭示了低维拓扑作为指导AI架构设计的新工具的潜力，并将结论推广至任意维度d > 3。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统神经网络研究常受宽度、深度和激活函数混杂影响，难以分离各因素作用。而高维空间中拓扑结构易被简化（如所有纽结在ℝ⁴中均为平凡），削弱了对网络行为的洞察力。因此，将表示空间限制在ℝ³，使拓扑结构保持非平凡性，有助于聚焦于深度与激活函数的影响，并提供可视化可能。

Method: 通过将网络每层的宽度固定为3（即输入输出为ℝ³），利用低维拓扑不变量（主要为链接数）追踪网络变换过程中拓扑性质的变化。采用理论证明与实验验证相结合的方式，对比不同架构（前馈网络、ResNet、transformer）及不同激活函数（单调/非单调）对链接数变化的能力。进一步将结果从d=3推广到任意d>3。

Result: 1. ResNet的跳跃连接与transformer的注意力机制在改变链接数方面具有相同表达能力；2. ResNets和transformers严格强于使用单调激活的前馈网络；3. 单调激活的前馈网络强于可逆与流模型；4. 非单调激活可使前馈网络提升至与ResNet和transformer同等级的表达能力。

Conclusion: 低维拓扑可以作为理解神经网络表达能力的有力工具，尤其在分离深度、宽度与激活函数影响方面具有独特优势。本研究为神经网络架构设计提供了新的理论视角，并揭示了非单调激活在增强模型表达力中的关键作用。

Abstract: We study layered models, including feedforward networks, ResNets, and transformers, by limiting each layer to a width of $d = 3$, i.e., $\mathbb{R}^3$ as representation space. This allows us to track how a neural network changes low-dimensional topological invariants through its layers. Just about any topological structure may be simplified or even trivialized by simply increasing dimension; e.g., any knot is equivalent to an unknot in $\mathbb{R}^4$. By restricting to $\mathbb{R}^3$, we not only isolate the effects of activation and depth from that of width, we work in a space that lends itself to easy visualization. We focus on linking number here, deferring other invariants like link groups, Milnor's $\barμ$-invariants, knot types, ambient cobordisms, to a sequel. We provide full proofs and empirical experiments to justify the following insights: When measured by their power to effect changes in linking numbers, the layer-skipping feature in ResNets is as powerful as the attention mechanism in transformers; both ResNets and transformers are strictly more powerful than feedforward neural networks with monotonic activations, which are in turn more powerful than invertible and flow-based models; but replacing monotonic activation with a nonmonotonic one elevates a feedforward network into the same expressivity class as ResNets and transformers. These results suggest that low-dimensional topology can be a useful tool to guide designs of AI architectures. We also generalize our results from $d = 3$ to arbitrary $d > 3$.

### [353] [SemRF: A Semantic Reference Frame for Residual-Stream Dynamics in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32022)
*Jian Gu,Aldeida Aleti,Chunyang Chen,Hongyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出语义参考系（SemRF），一种基于锚点的框架，用于分离语义测量与残差动态，解决语言模型深度计算中因读出坐标不一致导致的测量漂移问题。通过伪逆绑定实现精确同步，在受限双可逆性条件下获得稳定语义基坐标、失真界和近恒等变化。固定参考系后，残差计算变为深度语义轨迹。锚点诱导语义Voronoi图，距离或置信度将各层分配至粗粒度区域，同时保留区域内运动与边界信息。定义了层间步长、贡献谱和不平衡诊断，并引入松弛边距管以刻画轨迹约束；最小作用路径为管内唯一解，满足离散样条方程。作用过剩控制步长、曲率与谱失配；低曲率意味着分段线性可压缩性和局部知识密度高，轨迹复杂度低对应更少语义节点。通过参数到轨迹映射，揭示参数效率的条件关联：在符合数据拟合的前提下，低作用与低复杂度轨迹使用更少语义自由度。理论保证依赖于可控接口误差与显式管约束下的小投影残差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有残差流分析在深层语言模型中面临中间解码时读出坐标跨层不一致的问题，导致看似的语义演化可能实为测量漂移而非真实计算过程。为准确追踪语言模型内部语义动态，亟需一种能分离测量与动力学、保持坐标一致性且具备理论保障的分析框架。

Method: 提出语义参考系（SemRF），利用锚点固定语义基准，通过伪逆绑定实现层间精确同步；基于受限双可逆性假设，构建稳定语义基坐标系统；引入语义Voronoi图对层进行粗粒度划分，保留层内运动细节；定义层间步长、贡献谱、不平衡诊断及边距松弛管；以最小作用路径作为最优轨迹，其存在性与唯一性由二次加权正定性保证，并满足离散样条方程。

Result: SemRF框架实现了语义测量与残差动态的解耦，提供稳定坐标、可解释的轨迹结构与理论保证。最小作用路径具有唯一性，且低曲率轨迹表明系统具有分段线性可压缩性与高局部知识密度。通过参数-轨迹映射，揭示了低动作量与低复杂度轨迹对应更优的参数效率，即使用更少语义自由度即可建模有效信息。

Conclusion: SemRF为理解语言模型深层语义演化提供了新范式，不仅克服了传统方法中的测量漂移问题，还建立了从轨迹复杂度到参数效率的理论联系，为模型压缩、可解释性分析与设计新架构提供坚实基础。

Abstract: Residual-stream analysis asks how language-model computation evolves across depth, but intermediate decoding requires comparable readout coordinates across layers. If embedding anchors and unembedding readout disagree on the chosen span, apparent motion may reflect measurement drift rather than computation. We introduce \emph{Semantic Reference Frames} (SemRF), an anchor-based formalism separating semantic measurement from residual dynamics. A SemRF fixes anchors and measures states against them. Pseudo-inverse tying gives exact synchronization; under restricted bi-invertibility, SemRF yields stable semantic-basis coordinates, distortion bounds, and near-identity changes. With the frame fixed, residual computation becomes a depthwise semantic trajectory. The anchors induce a semantic Voronoi diagram: distance, or evidence such as logits, assigns each layer to a coarse cell, while coordinates retain within-cell motion and margins. We define layerwise steps, contribution profiles, and imbalance diagnostics, then use the Voronoi trace to define a margin-relaxed tube. The canonical trace is the minimum-action path inside this tube; when nonempty with positive quadratic weight, it is unique and obeys a discrete spline equation away from active constraints. Excess action controls step, curvature, and profile mismatch. Low curvature implies piecewise-linear compressibility and local knowledge density: lower trace complexity means fewer semantic knots. Through the parameter-to-trajectory map, this gives a conditional link to parameter efficiency: among admissible settings fitting data, lower-action and lower-complexity traces use fewer semantic degrees of freedom. The guarantees require controlled interface error and small projection residual under explicit tube constraints.

</details>


### [354] [QVal: Cheaply Evaluating Dense Supervision Signals for Long-Horizon LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32034)
*Sergio Hernández-Gutiérrez,Matteo Merler,Ilze Amanda Auzina,Joschka Strüber,Ameya Prabhu,Matthias Bethge*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出QVal，一个无需训练的测试平台，用于直接评估密集监督信号的质量。通过衡量方法得分与强参考策略的Q值对齐程度，实现不同方法在相同基准上的公平比较，避免了训练工程干扰。在21种密集监督方法、4个环境、7类方法族上进行大规模实验，发现简单提示基线表现优于许多新方法，且性能高度依赖方法族。该框架可扩展至新环境和方法，支持研究者在训练前迭代优化监督信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前密集监督方法缺乏统一、公平的评估基准，现有评估方式依赖下游性能，成本高且受训练工程因素干扰，导致不同方法难以直接比较。需要一种无需训练的测试方法来独立评估监督信号质量。

Method: 提出QVal，基于参考策略的Q值评估各方法对状态-动作对的评分是否与最优排序一致（即Q对齐），从而衡量监督信号的有效性。通过构建标准化测试环境与多模型验证，实现跨方法、跨模型、跨环境的可比性评估。

Result: 21种密集监督方法在多个环境和模型上测试显示：简单提示基线持续优于复杂方法；性能显著聚类于方法族内，不受模型规模、环境或观测模态影响。表明监督信号质量具有系统性差异，且可被提前识别。

Conclusion: QVal提供了一种高效、通用的评估框架，能有效分离监督信号质量与训练工程因素，揭示现有方法的实际差距，并支持研发者在训练前优化监督设计，推动密集监督研究向更透明、可复现的方向发展。

Abstract: LLM agents increasingly act over long horizons, where a single trajectory can contain hundreds or thousands of actions. In these settings, outcome-only rewards provide too sparse guidance, failing to inform the model about the goodness of intermediate actions. Dense supervision methods aim to solve this problem by scoring intermediate steps, from intrinsic confidence to self-distillation and embedding similarities. However, it is common practice to evaluate them by measuring the downstream performance of a training pipeline that integrates them. This is expensive, conflates supervision quality with training engineering confounders, and renders different methodological families requiring distinct training setups incomparable. As a result, dense supervision methods are rarely benchmarked on common ground. We introduce QVal, a training-free testbed for directly evaluating dense supervision signals. Given a state-action pair, QVal measures how well a method's score is Q-aligned: whether it orders actions according to the Q-values of a strong reference-policy. This lets us compare signals before any training run and separate signal quality from other engineering choices. We instantiate QVal as QVal-v1.0, benchmarking 21 dense supervision methods across four diverse environments and seven methodological families, with over 1.2K evaluation experiments across six open-weight model backbones. We find that simple prompting baselines consistently outperform recent dense supervision methods from the literature, and that performance clusters strongly by family. These findings hold across model sizes, environments, and observation modalities. QVal is designed to be easily extensible to new environments and methods, enabling researchers to iterate on dense supervision methods before any training run.

</details>


### [355] [Sequential RC-TGAN: Generating Relational Time Series with Spectral Envelope Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31904)
*Mohamed Gueye,Yazid Attabi,Manuel Morales,Maxime Dumas*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准编码方法如one-hot无法捕捉类别时间序列中的季节性与周期性等频域特征，且缺乏对关系型时序数据的有效生成与评估标准。

Method: 提出Seq. RC-TGAN，结合频谱包络理论设计可微损失函数以优化周期结构；采用变分高斯混合模型（VGM）对连续时间序列进行离散化处理；构建基于参数α的模拟类别时间序列作为基准；提出谱密度发散与谱包络发散两个新评估指标。

Conclusion: Seq. RC-TGAN成功实现了对复杂时序动态关系数据库的高质量合成，填补了频域保真度评估的空白，为关系型时序数据生成提供了新的有效框架。

Abstract: The generation of synthetic relational databases often involves modeling complex temporal dynamics, such as transaction logs or event sequences. A significant challenge in this domain is the handling of categorical time series (e.g., status codes), where standard encoding methods like one-hot encoding fail to capture intrinsic frequency-domain features such as seasonality and cyclicity. In this paper, we introduce Sequential RC-TGAN (Seq. RC-TGAN), a temporal extension of the RC-TGAN framework, equipped with a novel integrated loss function based on the \textit{Spectral Envelope Theory}. This differentiable loss allows the generator to directly optimize the preservation of latent periodic structures via backpropagation. While spectral envelope theory is inherently designed for categorical sequences, we extend this frequency-domain regularization to continuous time series by employing a Variational Gaussian Mixture Model (VGM) discretization strategy. To establish a mathematically rigorous evaluation standard, we simulate categorical time series governed by a parameter $α$, with exactly known theoretical spectral envelopes. Integrating these dynamic sequences into the child tables of a relational database yields a robust ground-truth benchmark for evaluating the frequency-domain fidelity of our generative framework. Furthermore, we address the lack of robust evaluation standards for relational time series by proposing two new metrics: Spectral Density Divergence and Spectral Envelope Divergence. Experimental results on real-world datasets, as well as our simulated benchmarks, demonstrate that our end-to-end approach significantly outperforms state-of-the-art systems in reproducing cyclic patterns and long-term seasonality across both categorical and continuous features.

### [356] [Interface-Aware Neural Newton Preconditioning for Robust Cohesive Zone Model Simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31921)
*Zhangyong Liang,Huanhuan Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向复杂界面断裂模拟的神经牛顿预处理器（IA-NNP），用于解决传统隐式有限元分析中粘聚力模型（CZM）因软化导致的收敛难题。该方法通过学习状态相关的界面修正，替代人工牛顿-拉夫森（NR）调整，保持原始牵引-分离律和求解框架不变。分为两种实现：初始猜测提升（IA-NNP-Init）与迭代级非线性右预处理（IA-NNP-NL），利用界面图特征（如开度、牵引力、切线、损伤状态等）进行可信赖的、有界修正，并确保仅通过原始CZM牛顿求解接受更新。理论证明其路径等价性——不改变离散解集但改善收敛路径。在多个基准测试中，相比标准NR与人工调整，显著提升困难增量的收敛率、分支恢复能力，减少失败次数，同时精确保留力-位移响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统粘聚力模型在隐式静态有限元分析中因软化行为常引发负切线、解跳变和牛顿盆地错配，导致收敛停滞、错误分支或反复步长削减；现有补救措施如黏性正则化、路径跟踪、动态松弛或人工牛顿调整，或改变有效响应、增加计算成本，或依赖经验规则，缺乏通用性和保真性。因此亟需一种既能保持物理一致性又能提升收敛鲁棒性的新方法。

Method: 提出界面感知神经牛顿预处理器（IA-NNP），将人工牛顿调整转化为基于规则的界面抬升，并推广为可学习的状态依赖修正。采用图神经网络建模界面状态特征（包括开度、牵引力、切线、损伤/历史变量、模式混合度、残差及邻近状态），生成有界且置信度控制的修正量。修正仅作用于活跃界面变量，且必须通过原始粘聚力模型牛顿求解验证后才被采纳。提供两种实现：IA-NNP-Init（初始猜测修正）与IA-NNP-NL（迭代级非线性右预处理）。

Result: 在水平、圆形、双界面及活动前缘等多种基准问题上，IA-NNP显著提升困难增量的收敛成功率，改善分支恢复能力，减少求解失败次数。相比标准牛顿法和人工调整，保持相同的力-位移响应，未引入额外耗散或改变原模型解集。

Conclusion: IA-NNP成功将人工经验规则转化为可学习、自适应的状态依赖修正机制，在不破坏原始物理模型的前提下，有效克服粘聚力模型中的收敛障碍，具备良好的通用性、保真性和鲁棒性，适用于复杂复合材料结构的界面断裂仿真。

Abstract: Cohesive Zone Models (CZMs) are widely used to simulate interface fracture, delamination, adhesive failure, and fiber--matrix debonding in aerospace composite structures. In implicit quasi-static finite element analyses, cohesive softening may introduce negative interface tangents, solution jumps, and Newton-basin mismatch, so the previous converged state can become a poor initial guess for the next increment. This may lead to stagnation, wrong-branch convergence, or repeated step cuts. Existing remedies, including viscous regularization, path following, dynamic relaxation, and manual Newton--Raphson (NR) modification, either alter the effective response, increase cost, or rely on hand-crafted interface rules. This work proposes an Interface-Aware Neural Newton Preconditioner (IA-NNP) for difficult CZM increments. IA-NNP recasts manual NR modification as rule-based interface lifting and generalizes it into a learned, state-dependent interface correction. The method acts only on active interface variables and preserves the original traction--separation law, residual assembly, tangent evaluation, history update, and dissipation checks. Two realizations are developed: IA-NNP-Init for learned initial-guess lifting and IA-NNP-NL for iteration-level nonlinear right preconditioning. Interface graph features encode opening, traction, tangent, damage/history variables, mode mixity, residuals, and neighboring states. The correction is bounded, confidence-gated, and accepted only through the original CZM Newton solve. A root-equivalence property shows that IA-NNP changes the path to convergence but not the discrete CZM solution set. Tests on horizontal, circular, two-interface, and active-front benchmarks show improved difficult-increment convergence, better branch recovery, and fewer failures than standard NR and manual NR modification, while preserving the force--displacement response.

</details>

Inspired by Model Autophagy Disorder (MAD), we introduce MADreMIA, a model-agnostic framework that enhances white-, gray-, and black-box MIA and DI. ### [359] [Radial Suppression Accelerates Algorithmic Generalization: A Geometric Analysis of Delayed Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32000)
*Srijan Tiwari,Aditya Chauhan,Manjot Singh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究神经网络在算法训练数据上记忆与泛化之间的延迟现象，提出通过径向膨胀的几何机制解释该延迟。通过激活空间的径向-角度分解，提出三个可验证假设：(i) 抑制径向膨胀会引入各向异性、依赖数据的权重正则化；(ii) 降低径向梯度能量至各向同性随机基线以下，促使主要进行角度更新；(iii) 偏向收敛到更平坦的极小值。实验采用单一超参数的范数惩罚，将激活限制在√d半径的超球面上，在模运算任务中使‘领悟’（grokking）速度提升最高达6倍，并在3位数加法任务中将1000万参数的nanoGPT训练步数减少一半。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出径向-角度分解的激活空间动力学模型，设计一种软约束范数惩罚，将激活控制在√d半径的超球面上，以抑制径向膨胀，并基于此构建理论推导和实验验证框架。

Result: 在模块化算术和3位数加法任务中，所提方法显著加速了‘领悟’过程，最大提速6倍；同时减少训练步数约50%，并验证了理论假设的正确性。

Conclusion: 交叉熵优化下的径向膨胀是导致记忆-泛化延迟的关键因素；通过抑制径向膨胀，可引导网络更早发现数据中的结构性规律，实现更快泛化。该研究为理解深度学习中的归纳偏置提供了新的几何视角。

Abstract: Why do neural networks memorize algorithmic training data long before they generalize? We present a geometric case study demonstrating that, on tasks where generalization requires discovering structured low-dimensional circuits, the memorization-generalization delay is driven by radial inflation of hidden representations under cross-entropy optimization. We formalize a radial-angular decomposition of activation-space dynamics and derive three testable propositions: (i) that penalizing radial inflation induces anisotropic, data-dependent weight regularization; (ii) that it suppresses radial gradient energy below the isotropic random baseline, forcing predominantly angular updates; and (iii) that it biases convergence toward flatter minima. To empirically validate these propositions, we study a single-hyperparameter norm penalty that softly constrains activations to a sqrt(d)-radius hypersphere. On modular arithmetic, this penalty accelerates grokking up to 6x across MLPs and Transformers, and halves training steps for a 10M-parameter nanoGPT on 3-digit addition.

### [360] [Surrogate Fidelity: When Can Open LLMs Explain Closed Ones?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32008)
*Philippe Chlenski,Zachariah Carmichael,Ayush Warikoo,Chia-Tse Shao,Yingxiao Ye,Aobo Yang,Vivek Miglani,Nehal Bandi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在无法访问模型内部机制的情况下，如何通过开放模型的代理测量来推断封闭模型的行为。研究发现，尽管预测结果高度一致，但归因（why）层面的差异显著，表明仅凭预测一致性无法保证机制解释的有效性。白盒信号（如注意力模式）虽稳定但对因果归因预测能力弱，而黑盒输入消融法更有效捕捉因果关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决在缺乏对语言模型内部结构完全访问权限时，如何利用开放模型的代理测量推断封闭模型行为的问题，特别是评估这些代理测量在预测、归因和表征层面的可靠性。

Method: 在十一款跨四个家族（Llama, Qwen, GPT, Gemini）的语言模型上，比较预测一致性、归因一致性和表征一致性；使用对数几率作为可兼容的标量读出，采用留一法归因分析模型行为，并对比白盒信号与黑盒输入消融的效果。

Result: 预测一致性远高于归因一致性，表明模型在答案上可能一致，但在决策原因上存在显著分歧；白盒信号（如注意力图、扰动幅度）虽在不同模型间稳定，但对因果归因的预测能力较弱；黑盒输入消融法更能准确捕捉因果关系。

Conclusion: 机制解释不能自动迁移到封闭模型，仅靠预测层面的一致性不足以支持这种迁移。研究强调需要谨慎对待基于开放模型的机制洞察在闭源模型上的适用性。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability (MI) requires full access to model internals, yet the APIs for most widely deployed language models at best expose log-probabilities over output tokens. This creates a surrogate problem: when do measurements made on open models allow us to make claims about a closed model? We evaluate surrogate fidelity at the prediction, attribution, and representation levels. For binary classification tasks, log-odds provide an API-compatible scalar readout of the model's representation space, and leave-one-out attributions provide insight into model behavior. Across eleven models spanning four families (Llama, Qwen, GPT, and Gemini), we find that prediction fidelity substantially overstates attribution fidelity: models that agree on what the answer is often disagree on why. We document an access-validity inversion: white-box signals like attention patterns and perturbation magnitudes are highly stable across models but only weakly predictive of causal attributions, which black-box input ablations capture by design. Mechanistic insight does not automatically transfer to closed targets, and prediction-level agreement is insufficient to warrant such transfer. Code and results are available at https://github.com/facebookresearch/surrogate.

### [361] [CoMet: Context and Multiplicity Decomposition for Multimodal Uncertainty Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32012)
*Sanghyuk Chun,William Yang,Amaya Dharmasiri,Olga Russakovsky*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不确定性估计在AI模型中长期存在挑战，尤其在多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）中更为复杂，因来源多样且答案可能无界。现有方法难以有效捕捉上下文与答案多样性之间的关系，亟需一种高效、精准的不确定性评估机制。

Method: 提出CoMet方法，将不确定性分解为两个部分：上下文特定项（反映任务/提示引起的模糊性）和多重性特定项（反映与输入兼容的多个合理答案的数量）。训练一个轻量级后处理不确定性模块来估计这两项，从而实现无需自回归生成或重复采样的高效不确定性估计。

Conclusion: CoMet为多模态大语言模型提供了一种高效且可解释的不确定性估计框架，能够有效捕捉上下文模糊性和答案多样性，具有广泛的应用潜力。

Abstract: Uncertainty estimation has been a long-standing challenge in AI models; it amounts to "knowing what you don't know," and metacognition is notoriously difficult even for humans (cf. the Dunning-Kruger effect). Although it is still far from solved even in simpler classification systems, tackling it in multimodal large language models (MLLMs) is becoming increasingly important. Within MLLMs, uncertainty can stem from any of the diverse sources as well as from their relationships, and further can stem from the unbounded answers in the open-ended setting. To tackle the issues, we propose CoMet, an MLLM uncertainty estimation method by decomposing uncertainty into a context-specific term and a multiplicity-specific term. The former captures ambiguity induced by the given context (e.g., task or prompt), while the latter captures how many plausible answers determined by the context remain compatible with the given input. We train a lightweight post-hoc uncertainty module to estimate these quantities, which enables efficient uncertainty estimation without autoregressive answer generation or repeated sampling. Experiments on various open-ended multimodal benchmarks, hallucination detection, and multiple-choice visual question answering benchmarks show that CoMet consistently improves uncertainty estimation over existing baselines while remaining efficient in practice. Code is available at https://github.com/princetonvisualai/comet_uncertainty

To bridge this gap, we propose FedLAB, a traceable semantic codebook framework that organizes multimodal graph knowledge into typed hierarchical codebooks for modality evidence, node semantics, and topology context. FedLAB further refines these trace units through federated semantic barycenter pre-training while keeping raw multimodal contents and graph structures local. Extensive experiments on 10 benchmarks and 6 downstream tasks show that FedLAB improves over state-of-the-art baselines by up to 7.53\%, while preserving a native semantic trace interface.

### [363] [TRIAGE: Role-Typed Credit Assignment for Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32017)

TL;DR: TRIAGE提出了一种基于语义角色的信用分配框架，通过引入角色类型来修正标准GRPO仅依赖最终验证结果的信用分配缺陷。该方法利用结构化判别器将每个动作段分类为决定性进展、有用探索、无进展基础设施或退化，并根据固定的角色条件规则生成分段奖励。这不仅保留了验证结果作为优化方向，还纠正了其在失败轨迹中惩罚探索、在成功轨迹中强化冗余行为的两大盲点。理论证明，角色条件信用是仅从角色标签可表达的最优分段校正，能降低优势估计误差并减少策略梯度方差。在ALFWorld、Search-QA和WebShop任务上，TRIAGE优于GRPO及其它基线模型，显著提升成功率，并减少环境交互次数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准GRPO仅使用最终验证结果作为统一优势信号，导致对探索行为的误罚和对冗余/退化行为的误激励，存在结构性缺陷。需要更精细的信用分配机制以准确反映各动作段的真实贡献。

Method: 提出TRIAGE框架，引入语义角色轴；使用结构化判别器对每个动作段进行四类标注（决定性进展、有用探索、无进展基础设施、退化）；基于角色标签设计固定规则生成分段过程奖励；理论分析表明该方法为角色标签下最优校正，能降低优势估计误差。

Result: 在ALFWorld、Search-QA、WebShop三个基准上，TRIAGE均优于GRPO，提升成功率；相比标量判别奖励与共享骨干值函数基线表现更优；消融实验显示收益主要来自角色类型而非单纯增加密集奖励；可靠识别成功轨迹中的退化行为是主要贡献，探索信用带来稳定次级收益；在完成的任务中，分别减少10.4%和14.8%的环境交互轮次。

Conclusion: TRIAGE通过角色类型化的信用分配，有效解决了传统结果导向信用的局限性，实现了更精准、低方差的策略学习，在多个复杂任务中显著提升性能并减少交互开销。

Abstract: Agentic reinforcement learning requires assigning credit to environment-facing actions such as searches, clicks, edits, navigation commands, and object interactions. Standard GRPO uses the final verifier outcome as a uniform advantage over all action tokens. This outcome signal is useful but structurally incomplete: it punishes useful exploration in failed rollouts and reinforces redundant or regressive actions in successful rollouts. We propose TRIAGE, a role-typed credit assignment framework that adds a semantic role axis to outcome credit. A structured judge classifies each segment as decisive progress, useful exploration, no-progress infrastructure, or regression, and a fixed role-conditioned rule maps these labels to bounded segment-level process rewards. This keeps verifier outcomes as the source of optimization direction while correcting the two main blind spots of outcome-only credit. We further show that role-conditioned credit is the optimal segment-level correction expressible from role labels alone -- a projection of the per-segment advantage residual onto the role variable -- so that the fixed role constants reduce advantage estimation error whenever the judge is reliable, and we connect this to lower-variance policy gradients. Across ALFWorld, Search-QA, and WebShop, TRIAGE improves success rates over GRPO for two policy models and outperforms both a scalar judge-derived process reward and an outcome-supervised shared-backbone value baseline. Ablations show that the gain comes from role typing rather than merely adding dense rewards: reliable detection of regression inside successful trajectories is the dominant contributor, while exploration credit provides a consistent secondary gain; on completed ALFWorld and WebShop rollouts, TRIAGE also reduces environment-facing turns by an additional $10.4\%$ and $14.8\%$ relative to GRPO.

</details>


### [364] [AdaJEPA: An Adaptive Latent World Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32026)
*Ying Wang,Oumayma Bounou,Yann LeCun,Mengye Ren*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AdaJEPA 是一种自适应的潜在世界模型，通过在模型预测控制（MPC）闭环中进行测试时适应，提升规划成功率。它在执行首个动作块后，利用观测到的状态转移作为自监督信号，更新模型并重新规划，无需额外专家示范。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有潜在世界模型在测试时通常保持冻结，当预测不准确或遇到分布偏移时，规划容易失败。需要一种能够在测试时动态调整模型的方法以提高鲁棒性。

Method: AdaJEPA 在 MPC 闭环中引入测试时自适应机制：执行初始动作后，利用实际观测的状态转移作为自监督信号，仅用一次梯度更新即刻调整模型参数，并基于更新后的模型重新规划。

Result: 在多种目标达成任务中，AdaJEPA 仅需每次重规划一步梯度更新，即可显著提升规划成功率，表现出强鲁棒性和高效性。

Conclusion: AdaJEPA 实现了无需额外示范的在线模型自适应，有效应对测试时分布偏移，显著增强潜在世界模型在复杂环境中的规划能力。

Abstract: Latent world models enable planning from high-dimensional observations by predicting future states in a compact latent space. However, these models are typically kept frozen at test time: when their predictions become inaccurate, planning can fail, especially under test-time distribution shift. To address this, we propose AdaJEPA, an adaptive latent world model that performs test-time adaptation within the closed loop of model predictive control (MPC). After training, AdaJEPA plans and executes the first action chunk, uses the observed next-state transition as a self-supervised adaptation signal, and replans with the updated model. This closed-loop update continuously recalibrates the world model without additional expert demonstrations. Across a range of goal-reaching tasks, AdaJEPA substantially improves planning success with as few as one gradient step per MPC replanning step.

</details>
